\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}

  \alnum{a} (vayxkitxyanunx) balvAgi KMDisu; ugarxTiVke mADu.

\bentry
\word[wag(1)]{wag} 
\pron{vAYxgf}

{\dictmeaning{
\sakirx\ (oMdu kaDeyiMda inonxMdakekx)
 alAlxDisu.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} alAlxDu. 
\num{2} (\pArxparx) (parxpaMca, kAl, \mo vugaLa \vi) hAgU hiVgU
naDeyutitxru: \eng{how wags the world?} heVge naDeyutitxde parxpaMca?
sithxtigatigaLu, vidayxmAnagaLu, heVgive?}} 
 
\noindent

jnaru ADikoLuLxtitxdAdxre. 
\num{2} \eng{dog wags tail} nAyi (saMtoVSa sUcisalu) bAl
alAlxDisutatxde. 
\num{3} \eng{the tail wags the dog} samAjda, yA pakaSxda kaniSaThx
vayxkitx samAjvanenxV, pakaSxvanenxV, ADisutAtxne, naDesutitxdAdxne,
alAlxDisutitxdAdxne; bAl nAyiyanenxV alAlxDisutitxde yA bAlda
pArupatayxvAgi hoVgide.

taleyalAlxDisu.}

\bentry
\word[wait(1)]{wait} 
\pron{veVTf} 
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} samaya kAyutitxru; sariyAda avakAshakAkxgi kAyutitxru: \eng{he
is waiting his opportunity} avanu sariyAda avakAshakAkxgi,
samayakAkxgi kAyutitxdAdxne. \eng{you must wait your turn} niVnu
ninanx saradigAgi kAyutitxrabeVku. \eng{wait my convenience} nanage
anukUlvAguvavaregU kAdiru, tALu.  
\num{2} (UT \mo vugaLigAgi beVrobabxra Agamanavanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx) 
kAdiru.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (kAyaR, parxyAN, \mo vugaLa \vi) (hesarisida kAlda yA
niriVkiSxsida GaTneyavaregU) taDe; tALu; kAyu; kAdiru: \eng{wait a
minute} oMdu nimiSa tALu. \eng{he waited (for) an hour} avanu oMdu 
GaMTe hotutx kAdidadx. \eng{I shall not wait any longer} nAnu inunx
muMde kAyuvudillx. \eng{he kept me waiting (\engit{or} he made me
wait)} avanu nananxnunx kAyuvaMte mADida. \eng{I have a month to wait
yet} nAnu inUnx oMdu tiMgaLa kAl kAdirabeVkAgide. \eng{I will do it
for you  while you wait} niVnu kAyutitxruvaSaTxralilx nAnu ninagAgi
adanunx mADutetxVne.  
\num{2} nidhAnisu; tALu; avasara paDabeVDa; taDe: \eng{wait till I
 come} nAnu baruvavaregU taDe, nidhAnisu. 
\num{3} eduru noVDu; niriVkiSxsu; kAyu: \eng{wait for high water}
kaDal ubabxrakAkxgi kAyutitxru. \eng{he waited to see what would
 happen} EnAguvudoV noVDoVNveMdu avanu kAdidadx. 
\num{4} rasetx \mo vugaLa pakakxdalilx savxlpxhotutx vAhanavanunx
nililxsu, `pAkfR' mADu. 
\num{5} 
\alnum{a} obabxra anukUl samayakAkxgi kAyu; veVLe kAyu. 

 \alnum{b} OleYsu; seVvisu. 

 \alnum{c} paricArike mADu; upacarisu. 

 \alnum{d} (gwravAthaR) BeVTi niVDu; dashaRna mADu; saMdashiRsu. 
\num{6} (\pArxparx) obabxna anucaranAgi, beMgAvalAgi, mayARdegAgi -- joteyalilx hoVgu. 
\num{7} anusarisi, anugatavAgi, PalvAgi -- baru, odagu, saMBavisu.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{he cannot wait} avanu kAyalAra; avanige tALemx illx. 
\num{2} \eng{that can wait} adanunx taDediDabahudu; adakekxVnU avasaravillx; adanunx kUDaleV mADabeVkAgillx. 
\num{3} \eng{wait and see} EneVnAgutatxdeyoV kAdu noVDutitxru. 
\num{4} \eng{wait at [\textit{or}} (\ame) \eng{on] table} UTda
meVjina baLi mANiyAgi yA paricArakanAgi vatiRsu, kAdiru. 
\num{5} \eng{wait for it!} (\AmA) 

  \alnum{a} adakAkxgi kAdiru! sariyAda kaSxN baruvavaregU adanunx pArxraMBisabeVDa. 

  \alnum{b} (aniriVkiSxtavAda yA soVjigada saMgatiyanunx heVLuvAga
keVLugarige kAtaravanunxMTumADalu heVLuva) savxlpx -- tALi, taDeyiri, heVLutetxVne (eMba mAtu). 
\num{6} \eng{wait for me!} nanagAgi kAdiru! nananxnunx biTuTx hoVgibiDabeVDa. 
\num{7} \eng{wait on} (\AseTxrXV\ matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf matutx
\kanu\ iMgalxMDf) tALemxyiMdiru; kAyu. 
\num{8} \eng{wait up} (obabxra Agamanavanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx)
ececxtitxru; niderx mADade yA malgade kAdiru. 
\num{9} \eng{wait (up)on} 

  \alnum{a} obabxna anukUlkAkxgi kAdiru. 

  \alnum{b} gaNyxvayxkitxge gwravasUcaka BeVTi niVDu. 
\num{10} \eng{you wait!} taDe, taDe! mADutetxVne! (shikiSxsutetxVneMba
bedarike).}

\bentry
\word[wall(1)]{wall} 
\pron{vAlf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (kalulx, iTiTxge, kAMkirxVTf, marada dimimx yA halge, \mo
vugaLiMda kaTiTxda, Uru, mane, koThaDi, gadedx, hol, toVT, \mo vanunx
parxteyxVkisuva) 
  
\alnum{a} goVDe; Bititx; kuDayx. 
  
\alnum{b} (AvaraNkAkxgi kaTiTxda) pwLi. 
  
\alnum{c} (deVvAlya \mo vugaLa) pArxkAra. 
  
\alnum{d} (rakaSxNegAgi kaTiTxda) koVTe (goVDe). 
  
\alnum{e} aDaDxgoVDe; muMde sAgalu aDiDxyAguva -- goVDe, taDe,
parxtibaMdhaka: \eng{we must break down the walls between community
and community} jAtijAtigaLa naDuvaN aDaDxgoVDegaLanunx,
aDiDxgaLanunx, nAvu oDeduhAkabeVku. 
\num{2} (citarxgaLu \mo vanunx parxdashiRsuva koThaDi, \mo vugaLa) goVDe.
\num{3} (noVTkekx yA pariNAmadalilx) goVDeyaMtiruva vasutx; kuDayxpArxyavAdadudx: 
  
\alnum{a} pavaRtada kaDidAda pAshavxR. 
  
\alnum{b} rakaSxNe: \eng{a wall of steel bayonets} ukikxna saniVnugaLa kApugoVDe, rakaSxNA sAlu. 
  
\alnum{c} aDataDe: \eng{a wall of indifference} upeVkeSxya taDegoVDe, taDegaTuTx.
\num{4} (oLage ToLALxgiruva yAvudeV vasutxvina yA racaneya) horameY; Bititx.
\num{5} (\aMrashA, \pArxvi\ matutx \savi) aMga, jiVvANu, \mo vugaLa --
Bititx, koVsha, pore, horapadara. 
\num{6} (\Kani) (loVhada eLe yA gereyanunx oLagoMDa) AvaraN shile; horashile.
\num{7} (\pArxparx) (rasetxya kAluhAdiyalilx) goVDeya pakakx (caraMDiya pakakxvallx).
\num{8} rasetxya pakakx, badi (naDurasetxyalalx).}}

\noindent

\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{bang (\engit{or} run) one's head against a (brick) wall} goVDege
talebaDiduko; asAdhayxvAdadadxkekx parxyatinxsu, keYhacucx.  
\num{2} \eng{blank wall} bariya goVDe; KAli goVDe; kada, horabAgilu, kiTki, \mo vu illxda yA alMkaraNgaLillxda goVDe.
\num{3} \eng{(drive \engit{or} send person) up the wall} (\AmA) (obabxnanunx)
reVgisu, keraLisu, talekeDisu. 
\num{4} \eng{give (person) the wall} (obabxrigobabxru edurAdAga, obabxnige) goVDeya pakakxvanunx (eMdare hecucx nimaRlvU surakiSxtavU Ada pakakxvanunx) biTuTxkoDu.
\num{5} \eng{go the wall} soVtu hoVgu yA mUle pAlAgu. 
\num{6} \eng{off the wall} (\ame) (\ashi) rUDhige virudadhxvAgi;
saMparxdAyabadadhxvAgirade. 
\num{7} \eng{see through a brick wall} alwkikavAda, loVkoVtatxravAda
-- oLagaNiNxru, aMtadaRqSiTx iru. 
\num{8} \eng{take the wall of} (obabxrigobabxru edurAdAga), obabxnige
goVDeya pakakxvanunx biTuTxkoDadiru (eMdare aSuTx swjnayxvanUnx
toVrisadiru). 
\num{9} \eng{the \hyperlink{writing pagu(2)}{writing} on the wall.}  
\num{10} \eng{up the wall} (\AmA) roVSaveVri yA talekeTTxMtAgi:
\eng{went up the wall when he heard it} adanunx keVLidAga
hucucxhucAcxda.  
\num{11} \eng{walls have ears} goVDegaLigU kivi ide; hoMci keVLuvavaru
idAdxre yA irabahudu. 
\num{12} \eng{with one's \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{back(1) nuga(30)}{${}^1$back} to the wall.}}

\bentry
\word[want(1)]{want} 
\pron{vAMTf} 
\gl{\nA} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} kore(yAgiruvudu); korate; nUyxnate; rAhitayx; aBAva: \eng{the
 ship is rotting for want of paint} baNNxvillxde A haDagu
koLeyutitxde. \eng{I took this for want of anything better} beVre
utatxmavAda yAvudU illxda kAraN nAnu idanunx hiDide. \eng{want of
 judgment} viveVcaneya korate yA aBAva. 
\num{2} Avashayxkate; agatayx; baDatana; dAridarxyX: \eng{he is in
 want of money} avanige haNda Avashayxkate ide, haN
agatayxvAgide. \eng{he is living in dire want} avanu
kaDubaDatanadalilx badukutitxdAdxne. 
\num{3} (badukige, suKkekx, jyakekx, korateyAgiruvudara pUreYkege
AvashayxkavAda vasutxvina) 
apeVkeSx; bayake; vAMCe yA bayasida vasutx: \eng{a man of few wants}
hecucx apeVkeSxgaLilalxda vayxkitx. \eng{this meets a long-felt want}
diVGaRkAldiMda anuBavisutitxdadx oMdu bayakeyanunx idu
niVgisutatxde. \eng{I can supply your wants} nAnu ninanx
agatayxgaLanunx pUreYsabalelx.} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word[want(2)]{want} 
\pron{vAMTf} 
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} illxdiru; aBAva hoMdiru; rahitavAgiru; korate, nUyxnate uLaLxdAdxgiru: \eng{the drawer wants a handle} arege hiDiyillx. 
\num{2} iMtiSuTx koreyAgiru.
\num{3} beVkAgiru; agatayxviru; AvashayxkavAgiru: \eng{he wants money} avanige haN beVkAgide. \eng{it wants doing} adanunx mADabeVkAgide.
\num{4} 
\alnum{a} bayasu; apeVkiSxsu; paDeyalu iSaTxpaDu, iciPxsu: \eng{I want
some sugar} nAnu savxlpx sakakxre bayasutetxVne. \eng{I want it done}
adanunx mADabeVkeMdu nAnu apeVkiSxsutetxVne. \eng{I want you to try}
niVnu parxyatinxsabeVkeMdu nAnu iciPxsutetxVne. 
 
\alnum{b} (\kanmu\ leYMgika BoVgakAkxgi vayxkitxyanunx) bayasu. 
 
\alnum{c} (\kanmu\ \birx) \kanmu\ nidiRSaTx riVtiya kAyaR bayasu, beVkAgiru: \eng{the garden wants weeding} toVTkekx kaLe kiVLabeVkAgide.}}

  \noindent 
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} korateyiru; aBAvaviru: \eng{let him want for nothing} avanige yAvudakUkx korateyillxdirali. 
 \num{2} (\ame, \AmA) (vayxvahAra, kirxye, \mo vugaLalilx) seVralu, toreyalu yA paDeyalu bayasu: \eng{I want to be out} nAnu toredu hoVga(lu) bayasutetxVne.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{do not want to} 

  \alnum{a} manasisxlalxdiru; iSaTxvillxdiru. 

  \alnum{b} mADalAgadu; mADabAradu: \eng{you don't want to overdo it} niVnu adanunx ati mADabAradu.
\num{2} \eng{wanted (by the police)} (aparAdhiyeMdu gumAni iruva kAraN) poliVsarige beVkAgidAdxne; poliVsaru (avananunx) huDukutitxdAdxre.}

\bentry
\word[war(1)]{war} 
\pron{vArf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} yudadhx; samara; saMgArxma; kadana; kALaga; raN: 

  \alnum{a} rASaTxrXrASaTxrXgaLige yA oMdeV rASaTxrXdalilx pakaSxpakaSxgaLige shasAtxrXsatxrXgaLiMda naDeyuva hoVrAT. 

  \alnum{b} yudadhxkAl; yudadhxda avadhi. 

  \alnum{c} yudadhx parisithxti; aMtArASiTxrXVya shAsana \mo vanunx sathxgitagoLisuvike.
\num{2} (\rUpa) 
  
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxgaLu, guMpugaLu, \mo vugaLa naDuvaN) vAyxjyx; jagaLa; kalha; saPxdheR; tikAkxT: \eng{war of words} vAguyxdadhx; mAtina jgaLa. 

  \alnum{b} (aparAdha, baDatana, roVga, \mo vugaLa virudadhx) hoVrAT; samara; nililxsade naDesuva caLavaLi.
\num{3} (\rUpa) neYsagiRka shakitxgaLa saMGaSaR.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{a good war} (\AmA) yudadhxda kAldalilx oMdu saMtoVSakaravAda avadhi.
\num{2} \eng{a holy war} pavitarxyudadhx; dhamaRyudadhx; dhAmiRka kAraNkAkxgi mADuva yudadhx.
\num{3} \eng{art of war} yudadhxkale; yudadhxsanAnxha taMtarxgaLu.
\hyperdef{W}{war(1)pagu(4)}{}
\num{4} \eng{at war} (shaturxgaLoDane) yudadhxdalilx toDagi, niratavAgi.
\num{5} \eng{carry the war into the enemy's camp (\engit{or} country)}
(\rUpa) parxtidALi naDesu; keVval AtamxrakaSxNeyalelxV taqpatxnAgade
parxtAyxroVpa \mo vanunx mADu. 
\num{6} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{council pagu(3)}{council} of war .} 
\num{7} \eng{declare war} yAvudeV rASaTxrX(gaLa) meVle yA (\rUpa) (saMsethx, padadhxti, \mo vugaLa meVle) yudadhx GoVSisu.
\num{8} \eng{dogs of war} (\kAparx) yudadhxda anAhuta, vinAsha.
\num{9} \eng{go to war} yudadhx hUDu; hoVrATvanunx AraMBisu, upakarxmisu. 
\num{10} \eng{go to the wars} (\pArxparx) seYnikanAgu; seYnika vaqtitxge seVru. 
\num{11} \eng{have been in the wars} (\AmA) yudadhxda gAya, hoDeta,
\mo vugaLa gurutugaLuLaLxvanAgiru. 
\num{12} \eng{laws of war} (shaturx kAyARcaraNege miti kalipxsalu
nAgarika janAMgagaLu aMgiVkarisiruva) yudadhxniyamagaLu;
yudadhxdhamaR. 
\num{13} \eng{private war} 
  
\alnum{a} (vayxkitxgaLalilx yA kuTuMbagaLalilx, kole \mo vugaLa shAsanagaLanunx lekikxsade, naDeyuva) vayxkitxkalha yA kuTuMbakalha. 

  \alnum{b} KAsagi yudadhx; beVroMdu rASaTxrXda nAgarikara meVle savxdeVshada sakARrada anumati illxde mADuva dALi, hoVrAT. 
\num{14} \eng{rights of war} yudadhxda hakukxgaLu; shAMtikAladalilx anAyxyaveMdu gaNneyAguva, Adare yudadhxkAldalilx yudadhxniratarige kelvu kAyaRgaLanunx mADalu anumati koDuva hakukxgaLu. 
\num{15} \eng{the War} Iga naDeyutitxruva yA ititxVcege mugida yudadhx. 
\num{16} \eng{trade of war} yudadhxda kasabau; seYnikavaqtitx. 
\num{17} \eng{war of \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{attrition pagu}{attrition}.} 
\num{18} \eng{war of the elements} (\kAparx) neYsagiRka shakitxgaLa saMGaSaR; birugALigaLu, parxvAhagaLu, BUkaMpagaLu, \mo\ anAhutagaLu. 
\hyperdef{W}{war(1) pagu(19)}{}
\num{19} \eng{war of nerves} (edurALiya manaHsethxYyaRvanunx karxmakarxmavAgi hALumADuva) dhaqtigeVDi yudadhx; sethxYyaRnAshaka yudadhx. 
\num{20} \eng{Wars of the Roses} (\ca) yAkfR matutx laMkAsaTxrfgaLa naDuve, $15$ne shatamAnadalilx iMgelxMDinalilx naDeda aMtayuRdadhx (biLi matutx keMpu gulAbigaLiMda parxtinidhisalpxTTxdudx). \num{21} \eng{war to the knife} \kanmu\ vayxkitxvayxkitxgaLa naDuve kaTTxkaDeyavaregU naDeyuva, nidARkiSxNyxvAda hoVrAT.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[warrant(1)]{warrant} 
\pron{vAraMTf} 
\gl{\nA} 
\dictmeaning{ 
\num{1} adhikAra; AdhAra; parxmAN; samathaRne; yAvudeV kelsavanunx
mADalu adhikAra koDuva vayxkitx yA viSaya: \eng{you have no warrant
for this action} I kelsakekx ninage yAva AdhAravU illx, adhikAravU
illx. \eng{his promise, or order is our strength, our warrant} avana
vAgAdxna, yA apapxNe, namamx bal, namamx AdhAra. \eng{I will be your
warrant} nAnu ninage AdhAravAgirutetxVne, adhikAra
koDuvavanAgirutetxVne. \eng{with warrant of a good conscience}
shudadhxvAda aMtasAsxkiSxya samathaRneyiMda. 
\num{2} vAraMTu: 
  
\alnum{a} pAvati, salilxke -- patarx. 

  \alnum{b} (haNvanunx paDedukoLaLxlu) liKita adhikAra patarx, apapxNe:
\eng{dividend warrant} DiviDeMDanunx paDeyalu liKita adhikArapatarx.  

  \alnum{c} sarakugaLanunx paDedukoLaLxlu yA odagisalu, seVvegaLanunx paDedukoLaLxlu yA odagisalu liKita adhikAra patarx, rahadAri: \eng{travel warrant} parxyANda rahadAri. 

  \alnum{d} serehiDiyalu, mane, meY, \mo vanunx shoVdhisalu adhikAra patarx, rahadAri. 

  \alnum{e} (mokadadxme hUDiruvavana parxtiyAgi kaTTxLe naDesalu) vakAltutxnAme; vakiVlnige koTiTxruva adhikArapatarx. 

  \alnum{f} seVvAvadhiyiMda, seVvAvadhiya baldiMda, adhikArakekx
baMdiruva adhikAriya adhikAra sAthxnada parxmANapatarx, saTiRphikeVTu.} 
\eentry

 iniquity} nananx pApagaLanunx toLedu parishudadhxgoLisu. 
\num{3} (kale, koLe, \mo vanunx) toLeduhAku; toLedu hoVgalADisu. 
\num{4} keY, bAyi, \mo vanunx toLeduko. 
\num{5} toVyisu; neneyisu; AdarxRgoLisu; odedxmADu: \eng{roses washed

\num{6} (nadi, samudarx, \mo vugaLa \vi) niVru (kare, daDa, tiVra, \mo
vanunx) tAgu; baDi; toLe. 
\num{7}

kocicxkoMDu hoVgu; dUDikoMDu hoVgu: \eng{a wave washed him overboard}
oMdu ale avananunx haDaginiMda (kaDalige) kocicxhAkitu. \eng{he was
 washed up by the sea} avanu samudarxdiMda meVlkekx (tiVrakekx)
dUDalpxTTx.

sameduhoVda koVDugalulxgaLu. 
 
\alnum{c} toVDu; koreduhAku: \eng{water had washed a channel} niVru
oMdu kAluveyanunx koreduhAkitutx, toVDitutx. 
\num{8} aduranunx -- toLe, jAlADu; niVriniMda toLedu aduriniMda
loVhavanunx beVpaRDisu. 
\num{9} (kAgada, goVDe, \mo vugaLa meVle) teLuvAgi baNNx -- baLi, toDe,
savaru, leVpisu. 
\num{10} (kiVLuloVhagaLige cinanx \mo vugaLa) mulAmu -- hAku, leVpisu.}}

\bentry

\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{

toLedukoLaLxbeVku, sAnxna mADabeVku. 
\num{2} ogeyabeVkAda, ogeyutitxruva baTeTxgaLu.
\num{3} niVrina harivu yA sapapxLa (\kanmu\ niVrinalilx pAterxya yA haDagina calnadiMdAguva alegaLa sadudx).
\num{4} (calisutitxruva vimAnada hiMdina) hiMgALi; raBasada gALi.

\bentry
\word[water(1)]{water} 
\pron{vATrf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} niVru; jl; vAri; paya; udaka; aMbau; shara: 

  \alnum{a} pAradashaRkavAda, vAsaneyillxda, ruciyillxda (Akisxjnf
matutx heYDorxjnfgaLa) darxvasaMyukatx (rAsAyanika sUtarx,
\eng{H$_2$O}). 

  \alnum{b} samudarx, saroVvara, nadi, maLegaLa matutx jiVvigaLu
sarxvisuva, jlAMshaviruva darxva. 

  \alnum{c} (samudarx, nadi,
saroVvara, \mo) niVru; niVrina haravu; jlrAshi. 
\num{2} (\bava dalilx) jlBAga; jl parxdeVsha; samudarxda yA nadiya
BAga: \eng{in Icelandic waters} aisfleMDina jlBAgadalilx. 
\num{3} (aneVkaveVLe \eng{the waters}) (Knijjlda UTe \mo vugaLalilxna)
Knij jl. 
\num{4} oMdu nidiRSaTx vasutxvina dArxvaN: \eng{lavender water}
lAYxveMDarf dArxvaN. 
\num{5} (vajrx \mo vugaLa \vi) niVru; pAradashaRkate matutx
ujjxvXlte. 
\num{6} darxva baMDavALa; SeVru hecacxLadiMda keYgArike yA vANijyx
saMsethxya nAmamAtarx baMDavALavanunx hecicxsuvudariMda seVrida
baMDavALada motatx.}} 
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{by water} jlmAgaRvAgi; haDagu \mo vugaLa mUlka. 
\num{2} \eng{cast one's bread upon the waters} kaqtajacnxteyanAnxgali
parxtiPalvanAnxgali bayasade satakxmaR mADu. 
\num{3} \eng{in deep water(s)} kaSaTxgaLalilx toLalutatx; saMkaTkekx
sikikx. 
\num{4} \eng{make water} 

\alnum{a} mUtarxvisajiRsu.
 
\alnum{b} (haDagina \vi) niVru oLakekx nugugx yA horakekx soVru. 
\num{5} \eng{of the first water}

  \alnum{a} atuyxtatxma, atuyxtakxqqSaTx -- guNda: \eng{diamond of the
 first water} atuyxtakxqqSaTx vajrx. \eng{genius of the first water}
savaRsherxVSaThx parxtiBe. 

  \alnum{b} (\hiV) atayxMta kiVLAda; heVyavAda: \eng{blunder of the the
 first water} atayxMta heVyavAda tapupx. 
\num{6} \eng{on the water} (\rUpa) doVNiyalilx yA haDaginalilx.
\num{7} \eng{pass water} mUtarxvisajiRsu.
\hyperdef{W}{water(1) pagu(8)}{}
\num{8} \eng{pour (\engit{or} throw) cold water on} taNiNxVreracu; yoVjne \mo
vanunx hiVyALisi nirutAsxhagoLisu; vayxkitxyanunx nirutAsxhagoLisu. 
\num{9} \eng{shed blood like water} rakatxvanunx niVrinaMte celulx;
dayAdAkiSxNyxvillxde kolulx. \num{10} \eng{spend money like water}
haNvanunx niVrinaMte celulx; dhArALavAgi, pariNAmavanunx lekikxsade
vecacxmADu. 
\num{11} \eng{water of life} AdhAyxtimxka jAcnxna. 
\num{12} \eng{waters of forgetfulness} visamxqqti yA maraN. 
\num{13} \eng{water under the bridge \engit{or} over the dam} maraLi bArada
gatakAl; kaLeduhoVda matutx matetx saripaDisalAgada GaTnegaLu.}

\bentry
\word[way(1)]{way} 
\pron{veV} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (ODADuva yA yAvudeV sathxLakekx hoVguva) rasetx; dAri; mAgaR;
patha (\rUpa\ saha): \eng{asked the way to Mysore} meYsUrige hoVguva
dAri keVLida. 
\num{2} (kaTTxDa \mo vugaLa oLakekx hoVguva yA Acege hoVguva) dAri:
\eng{could not find the way out} horakekx hoVguva dAri kANlillx,
sigalillx. 
\num{3} (udedxVshavoMdanunx sAdhisuva) vidhAna; karxma; riVti; yoVjne;
upAya: \eng{this is not the way to do it} adanunx mADuva vidhAna
idallx. \eng{there is a right way and a wrong way of using the
 tool} upakaraNvanunx baLasuva sariyAda riVti oMdide, tapu px riVti
oMdide. \eng{do it this way} adanunx hiVge, I riVti mADu. 
\num{4} sAdhakashakitx; obabxna udedxVshavanunx pUreYsuva, guriyanunx
sAdhisuva sAmathaRyx: \eng{he has a way with him} avanalolxMdu
visheVSa sAmathaRyxvide. 
\num{5} vayxkitxyobabxnige iSaTxvAda, avanu bayasida yA Ayekx mADida
-- kAyaRvidhAna, kAyaRriVti, mAgaR.  
\num{6} padadhxti; vADike; rUDhi; aBAyxsa; vataRne; naDevaLi;
havAyxsa; veYyakitxka veYlkaSxNyx: \eng{has a way of forgetting
 things} viSayagaLanunx maretubiDuva aBAyxsavide. \eng{it is not my
 way to deceive people} jnaranunx vaMcisuvudu nananx
padadhxtiyallx. \eng{things had a way of going badly} parisithxtigaLu
keTuTxhoVguvudu oMdu vADikeyAgitutx. \eng{he has a way of leaving
 the bills unpaid} bilulxgaLanunx pAvati mADadiruvudu avanadoMdu
rUDhi. 
\num{7} nidiRSaTx jiVvanakarxma yA nidiRSaTx kAyaRvidhAna: \eng{I
 soon got into his ways} nAnu beVga avana jiVvanakarxmagaLanunx
aritukoMDe. \eng{soon got into the way of it} beVga adara
kAyaRvidhAnagaLanunx kaMDukoMDe. 
\num{8} GaTnegaLu saMBavisuva sahaj -- karxma, riVti: \eng{that is
 always the way} GaTnegaLu saMBavisuvudu yAvAgalU aMteyeV, adeV
riVtiyalilxyeV. 
\num{9} parxyAN dUra; parxyAN mADida yA mADabeVkAda dUra: \eng{is a
 long way away} bahaLa dUradalilxde. 
\num{10} (muMduvareyalu) nirAtaMkavAda, aDiDxaDacaNegaLillxda --
avakAsha, dAri.  
\num{11} aDacaNegaLillxda -- eDe, jAga. 
\num{12} parxgatipatha; muMduvareyalu bayasuva yA sahajvAda -- mAgaR,
parxdeVsha. 
\num{13} (yAvudeV dikikxnalilx) munanxDe; muMduvarike; parxgati:
\eng{pushed my way through} nugigx dArimADikoMDu hoVde. \eng{fight
 one's way through} hoVrADutAtx oMdu sathxLada mUlka hoVgu.
\num{14} (haDagu \mo vugaLa) calna; karxmaN; yAna; sAguvike:
\eng{gather way} muMde yA veVgavAgi sAgu. \eng{lose way} nidhAnavAgi
sAgu; veVga tagigxsu. 
\num{15} 
\alnum{a} (sathxLadiMda sathxLakekx) parxyAN; hoVgutitxruvudu:
\eng{met him on the way home} manege hiMdirugutitxdAdxga dAriyalilx
kaMDe. 

  \alnum{b} parxyANkAl; parxyANdalilx kaLeda yA kaLeyuva kAl: \eng{with
 songs to cheer the way} parxyAN mADutAtx ulAlxsadiMdiralu
hADugaLanunx hADutatx. 
\num{16} nidiRSaTx dikukx; hesarisida kaDe: \eng{step this way} I kaDe
bA. \eng{which way are you going?} elilxge, yAva kaDege
hoVgutitxdidxVye? 
\num{17} (\bava dalilx) vasutxvoMdanunx oDeyabahudAda -- BAgagaLu,
viBAgagaLu: \eng{split it three ways} adanunx mUru BAgagaLAgi oDe. 
\num{18} (\AmA) yAvudaradeV -- vAyxpitx, keSxVtarx: \eng{want a few
 things in the stationery way} leVKnasAmagirxgaLige saMbaMdhisida
kelvu vasutxgaLu beVku. 
\num{19} (vayxkitxya) kasubau; vaqtitx; udoyxVga. 
\num{20} nidiRSaTx -- sithxti, parisithxti, avasethx, vidayxmAna:
\eng{things are in a bad way} parisithxti keTTxdAgide; vidayxmAnagaLu
duHsithxtiyalilxve. 
\num{21} aMsha; viSaya; guN: \eng{is useful in some ways} kelvu
aMshagaLalilx upayukatxvAgide. 
\num{22} (\bava dalilx) 

 \alnum{a} (hosa haDaganunx samudarxkekx iLisalu tolegaLu \mo
vugaLiMda racisida) jAruhAdi; iLAlu; iLakalu. 

 \alnum{b} yaMtarxvoMdanunx sarisalu baLasuva joVDikaMbi hAdi, mAgaR,
\mo vu.}} 
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{across (\engit{or} over) the way} edurina; edurubadiya; (\kanmu\
rasetxya) eduruBAgadalilxna: \eng{house across (\engit{or} over) the way}
edurumane; edurubadiya mane.
\hyperdef{W}{way(1)pagu(2)}{}
\num{2} \eng{all the way} iDiV dUra; pUtiRyAgi. 
\num{3} \eng{any way = \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{anyway(1)}{anyway}.}
\num{4} \eng{be on one's way} horaDu; dAri hiDi; horaTuhoVgu;
nigaRmisu. 
\num{5} \eng{by the way} 

 \alnum{a} pArxsaMgikavAgi; saMbaMdhisirada mAtanunx ADuvAga ADuva
mAtAgi. 

 \alnum{b} parxyANdalilx.
\num{6} \eng{by way of} 

 \alnum{a} mUlka; mAgaRvAgi: \eng{by way of Bangalore} beMgaLUrina
mUlka. 

 \alnum{b} adakekx badalAgi, parxtiyAgi; A rUpadalilx: \eng{carries a
 stick by way of a weapon} Ayudhakekx badalAgi koVlnunx
hiDididAdxne. \eng{did it by way of apology} kaSxmAyAcaneya
rUpadalilx adanunx mADida. 

 \alnum{c} udedxVshadiMda: \eng{by way of discovering the truth}
nijAMshavanunx kaMDuhiDiyuva udedxVshadiMda. 

 \alnum{d} kalipxsikoMDu yA toVpaRDisikoLuLxtatx: \eng{by way of
 making a great effort} BAri parxyatanxvanunx mADutitxruvaMte
kalipxsikoMDu yA toVrisikoLuLxtatx. 

 \alnum{e} mUlka; muKAMtara; A riVtiyalilx, vidhAnadalilx. 
\num{7} \eng{clear the way} 

 \alnum{a} aDetaDegaLanunx tegeduhAku; dAri sugamagoLisu. 

 \alnum{b} dAri biDu; pakakxkekx sari; saridu nilulx.
\num{8} \eng{come one's way} obabxna pAlige baru; obabxnige -- sigu, laBayxvAgu 
\num{9} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{feel(1) nuga(4)}{${}^1$feel} one's way.} 
\num{10} \eng{find a way} dAri kaMDuko; guri sAdhisuva mAgaRvanunx,
udedxVshasAdhaneya upAyavanunx kaMDuko. 
\num{11} \eng{find its (\engit{or} the \engit{or} one's) way} guri muTuTx;
udidxSaTxsAthxna talupu. 
\num{12} \eng{either way} eraDaralilx yAvudAdarU oMdu riVtiyalilx;
hiVgoVhAgoV; hiVgAdarU hAgAdarU. 
\hypertarget{way pagu13}{}
\num{13} \eng{get (\engit{or} have) one's way} tanage
beVkenisidadxnunx paDeduko; tananx udedxVsha sAdhisuvaMte, iSATxthaR
neraveVruvaMte noVDiko.  
\num{14}\eng{give way} 

 \alnum{a} taDeyalAradAgu; edurisalAgade hoVgu; maNi; bagugx. 

 \alnum{b} (beVrobabxnige) dAribiDu; eDekoDu; Adayxte, parxthamAvakAsha koDu. 

 \alnum{c} riyAyiti toVrisu, niVDu.

 \alnum{d} (kaTTxDa \mo vugaLa \vi) meVlina BAradiMda -- kusi; muridu
biVLu, bidudxhoVgu. 
\num{15} \eng{give way to} 

 \alnum{a} tananx sAthxnavanunx (beVrobabxnige yA beVroMdakekx)
biTuTxkoDu. 

 \alnum{b} (beVrobabx yA beVroMdu) tanagiMta meVlina sAthxnakekx
EruvaMte Agu; tanagiMta meVlina sAthxnavanunx (inonxbabxnige yA
inonxMdakekx) biTuTxkoDu. 

 \alnum{c} (BAva \mo vugaLige) vashavAgu; sharaNAgu; sAvxdhiVnavAgu. 

 \alnum{d} (aMbigara \vi) birusAgi huTuTx hAku. 
\num{16} \eng{go a person's way} obabxnu hoVgutitxruva dikikxgeV,
eDegeV hoVgu; obabxna jote, obabxnoDane hoVgu: \eng{are you going my
 way ?} niVnu nanonxDane, nAnu hoVgutitxruvalilxgeV hoVgutitxdidxVyA? 
\num{17} \eng{go one's way} 

 \alnum{a} horaDu; horaTuhoVgu; nigaRmisu. 

 \alnum{b} (GaTnegaLu, saMdaBaRgaLu, parisithxtigaLu, \mo vugaLa \vi)
(obabxnige) anukUl(kara)vAgiru. 
\num{18} \eng{go one's own way} (\kanmu\ itarara salhe, baudidhxvAda,
\mo vanunx lekikxsade, avugaLige virudadhxvAgi) tananxdeV dAri hiDi;
tanage toVridaMteyeV mADu; savxtaMtarxvAgi vatiRsu. 
\num{19} \eng{go
 out of one's way} (yAvudanenxV sAdhisalu, neraveVrisalu) visheVSa
parxyatanx mADu; rUDhiyAgiruvudakikxMta hecicxna mutuvajiR,
parisharxma vahisu; yAvudeV kAraN yA balvaMta illxde savxMta iceCxyiMda
vatiRsu: \eng{went out of their way to help} sahAya mADalu visheVSa
sharxmavahisidaru. 
\num{20} \eng{go the way of all good things} oLeLxya vasutxgaLaMte
anivAyaRvAgi aLi, nAshavAgu. 
\num{21} \eng{go the way of all earth
 (\engit{or} flesh \engit{or} nature)} sAyu. 
\num{22} \eng{go the whole (\engit{or} all the) way} (\AmA) pUtiR saMBoVga,
pUNRmeYthuna naDesu. 
\num{23} \eng{have a way} (yAvudanenxV mADalu) visheVSa kwshal yA
sAmathaRyx hoMdiru. 
\num{24} \eng{have a way with one} AkaSaRka matutx olisuva guN,
riVtiniVti hoMdiru. 
\num{25} \eng{have one's way with} (\hA) yAroDaneyAdarU saMBoVga
naDesu (\kanmu\ avara iSaTxkekx viroVdhavAgi eMba sUcaneyoDane). 
\num{26} \eng{have it \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{both(1) nuga(2)}{${}^1$both} ways.} 
\num{27} \eng{have it one's own way} = 
\hyperlink{way pagu13}{\pagu\ \eng{(13)}}.  
\num{28} \eng{have it your (own) way} (heVLidadxkekx yA sUcisidadxkekx
ollxda manasisxna opipxgeya utatxravAgi) niVnu heVLidaMteyeV Agali;
ninage toVridaMte mADu; nininxSaTx(daMte mADu). 
\num{29} \eng{in a (\engit{or} one) way (\engit{or} some ways)}
savxlpxmaTiTxge; tusu. 
\num{30} \eng{in a \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{big(1) nuga(3)}{${}^1$big} way.} 
\num{31} \eng{in a \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{fair(1) nuga(8)}{${}^1$fair} way.} 
\num{32} \eng{in a (\engit{or} the) \hyperref{kandict_f.pdf}{F}{family(1) nuga(1)}{${}^1$family} way.} 
\num{33} \eng{in a small way} saNNx parxmANdalilx; mahatAvxkAMkeSx
illxde. 
\num{34} \eng{in its way} adara riVtiyalilx; adakekx takukxdAda
nidiRSaTx daqSiTxkoVnadiMda noVDidare. 
\num{35} \eng{in more ways than one} oMdallx halvu -- athaRgaLalilx,
riVtigaLalilx. 
\num{36} \eng{in no way} yAva riVtiyalUlx allx; allxveV allx. 
\num{37} \eng{in one's (\engit{or} the) way} (obabxnige) aDiDxyAgi;
parxtibaMdhakavAgi. 
\num{38} \eng{keep (\engit{or} stay) out of someone's way} obabxnanunx
saMdhisadiru, BeVTi mADadiru. 
\num{39} \eng{lead the way} mAgaRdashaRna mADu: 

 \alnum{a} mAgaRdashaRkanAgi yA nAyakanAgi vatiRsu. 

 \alnum{b} (yAvudanenxV) mADuva vidhAnavanunx, heVge
mADabeVkenunxvudanunx toVrisu. 
\num{40} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{lion nuga(3)}{lion} in the way.} 
\num{41} \eng{look the other way} 

 \alnum{a} beVreDe noVDu; noVDabeVkAdudanunx biTuTx beVreDege muK
tirugisu; gamanisabeVkAdudanunx kaDegaNisu. 

 \alnum{b} (dAriyalilx BeVTiyAda) paricita vayxkitx \mo varanunx --
alkaSxyXmADu, upeVkiSxsu, kaDegaNisu; avariMda beVre dikikxge muK
tirugisu.  
\num{42} \eng{lose one's (\engit{or} the) way} 

 \alnum{a} dAri -- tapupx, kaLeduko; tapupxdAri hiDi. 

 \alnum{b} (\rUpa) dAritapupx; dumARgaRkekx biVLu. 
 \num{43} \eng{make (\engit{or} pay) its way} (udayxma, saraku, \mo vugaLa \vi)
lABadAyakavAgiru. 
\num{44} \eng{make one's (own) way (in the world)} (jiVvanadalilx)
muMduvari; ELige hoMdu; parxgati sAdhisu. 
\num{45} \eng{make way} 

 \alnum{a} muMduvari; muMde sAgu (\rUpa\ saha). 

 \alnum{b} dAri mADikoDu; muMde hoVgalu eDe mADikoDu. 
\num{46} \eng{not (\engit{or} nothing) out of the way} visheVSavAdudu EnU
allx; rUDhiyadakikxMta BinanxveVnU allx; mAmUlinadeV. 
\num{47} \eng{no way} adu asAdhayx. 
\num{48} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_o.pdf}{O}{once(1) pagu(3)}{${}^1$once} in a way (\engit{or} while).} 
\num{49} \eng{one way and another} (viSayada) viBinanx aMshagaLanunx,
vividha muKgaLanunx parigaNisidare. 
\num{50} \eng{one way or another} oMdallx oMdu riVtiyalilx; yAvudoV
oMdu riVtiyalilx. 
\num{51} \eng{only his etc. way} avana vicitarx, vilkaSxN riVti:
\eng{it is only his way} idu avana vicitarx riVti (adanenxVnU
gamanisabeVkAgillx, adakekxVnU mahatatx vx
koDabeVkAgillx). 
\num{52}\eng{on the (\engit{or} one's) way} 

 \alnum{a} dAriyalilx; parxyAN \mo vanunx mADutitxruvAga. 

 \alnum{b} muMduvaridu: kelsa muMduvaridu mugiyuva GaTTxkekx, hatitxra
baMdu. 

 \alnum{c} (\AmA) (kUsina \vi) gaBaRdalilxdudx inUnx jnisada,
horabarada; jnana samIpisutitxruva, hatitxravAgutitxruva. 
 \num{53} \eng{on the way out} (\AmA) 

 \alnum{a} horaTuhoVgutitxruva; nigaRmisutitxruva. 

 \alnum{b} iLimuKvAgutitxruva; sAthxna, gwrava, pirxVti
kaDameyAgutitxruva, kaLedukoLuLxtitxruva. 

 \alnum{c} (phAyxSaninxna
\vi) kaNmxreyAgutitxruva; nashisutitxruva. 
 \num{54} \eng{out of \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{harm(1) nuga}{harm's} way.} 
\num{55} \eng{out of one's way} tananx dAriyiMda Ace; tAnu
hoVgabeVkeMdiruva mAgaRdiMda Ace, dUravAgiruva. 
\num{56} \eng{out of the way} 

 \alnum{a} aDiDxyAgirada; taDeyAgirada. 

 \alnum{b} itayxthaRgoLisida; bageharida. 

 \alnum{c} (vayxkitxya \vi) serege hAkida yA kollxlpxTTx. 

 \alnum{d} (niSeVdhavAciyoDane) sAmAnayxvAda; mAmUligiMta hececxVnU Agirada. 

 \alnum{e} (sathxLada \vi) aBukatx mUleya; tiVra dUrada; talpalu
kaSaTxvAda; dugaRmavAda. 
\num{57} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{pave pagu}{pave} the way.} 
\num{58} \eng{pay one's way} vecacx tUgisu; vecacxkekx samavAda
AdAyaviru; sAlvAgadiru. 
\num{59} \eng{put a person in the way} (yAvudanenxV mADalu) obabxnige
avakAsha mADikoDu; Asapxda kalipxsu. 
\num{60} \eng{put oneself out of the way} inonxbabxnige upakAra
mADalu anagatayx toMdare tegedukoLuLxvike, ananukUl taMdukoLuLxvike. 
\num{61} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{see(1) pagu(23)}{${}^1$see} one's way clear to.} 
\num{62} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{step(1) pagu(10)}{${}^1$step} this way.} 
\num{63} \eng{take its (\engit{or} one's) way (to)} -ge yA -kaDege hoVgu 
\num{64} \eng{the other way about (\engit{or} round)} (sAthxna yA dikikxna
\vi) tirugamuruga; talekeLagAgi; hiMdumuMdAgi. 
\num{65} \eng{the way of the Cross} 

 \alnum{a} kUrxSAroVhaN citarxsherxVNi; yeVsuvina kUrxSAroVhaNda
GaTnegaLanunx citirxsiruva (\kanmu\ caciRnalilx iTiTxruva) citarxgaLa
sAlu, sherxVNi. 

 \alnum{b} shilubeya vadhasathxLakekx yeVsuvina payaN. 

 \alnum{c} kerxYsatxnobabxna duHKpUNR hAgU tAyxgada jiVvana. 
 \num{66} \eng{under way} 

 \alnum{a} (kAyaRda \vi) naDeyutitxru; sAgutitxru. 

 \alnum{b} (\rUpa) muMduvariyutitxru, munf sAgutitxru. 
 \num{67} \eng{way back} bahaLa hiMde; pArxciVna kAldalilx. 
\num{68} \eng{way of life} jiVvana mAgaR; jiVvana vidhAna;
vayxkitxgaLa kAyaRgaLu \mo\ ellxvanUnx niyaMtirxsuva tatatx vxgaLu yA
aBAyxsagaLu. 
\num{69} \eng{way of the world} loVka -- rUDhi, vADike; rUDhiya naDevaLike, AcAra vayxvahAra; jnagaLu sAdhAraNvAgi vatiRsuva, GaTnegaLu sAmAnayxvAgi saMBavisuva -- paripAT. 
\num{70} \eng{way of thinking} AloVcanA mAgaR; ciMtanavidhAna:
\eng{to one's way of thinking} obabxna AloVcaneya, aBipArxyada
parxkAra.

{\dictmeaning{}}

hAkiko; dharisu: \eng{wears green shorts} hasiru caDiDxyanunx
uDutAtxne. \eng{she intends to wear earrings} avaLu OlegaLanunx
dharisalu iciPxsutAtxLe. 
\num{2} sAmAnayxvAgi, vADikeyAgi -- uDu, toDu: \eng{wears green}
hasirubaTeTx uDutAtxne. 
\num{3} (deVhada meVle uDupinaMte yA aMgadaMte) dharisu; hAkiko; toDu:
\eng{wear a beard} gaDaDx biDu, beLesu. \eng{wear glasses}
kananxDaka hAkiko. \eng{wear hair long} talegUdalnunx udadxvAgi
iTuTxko. 
\num{4} (muKBAva yA rUpavanunx) taLe; tALu; toVru; parxdashiRsu;
parxkaTisu: \eng{wore a frown} siDukumoVre hAkidadx. \eng{wear a
 joyful face} saMtoVSada muKtoVru. \eng{wear a sour look} kahimoVre
hAku. \eng{the day wore a different aspect} dina BinanxmuK
toTiTxtutx. 
\num{5} (\birx)(\AmA)(\sA\ niSeVdhavAciyoDane) opupx; sahisu; tALiko:
\eng{they won't wear that excuse} avaru A sabaUbanunx opupxvudillx. 
\num{6} ujijx, otAtxya heVri yA baLasi yAvudaradeV meVlemxYyanunx -
hAnigoLisu, hALumADu, tUtubiVLisu, jiVNRgoLisu, kaqshagoLisu yA
BAgashaH aLisihAku: \eng{inscription has been worn} shAsana
aLisihoVgide. \eng{wear one's trousers into holes (\engit{or}
bagginess)} -- SarAyiyanunx uTuTxuTuTx tUtu biVLisu (yA dagale
mADu). \eng{worn to a stick with care} ciMteyiMda kaqshavAgi 
kaDiDxyAgidAdxne. \eng{toil-worn} duDimeyiMda biVLAgidAdxne. 
\num{7} saveyisu; teVyu; ujijxhAku: \eng{steps worn with pilgrims'
 feet} yAtirxkara kAlugaLiMda saveduhoVda meTiTxlugaLu. 
\num{8} susutx biVLisu; AyAsagoLisu; daNisu; baLalisu. 
\num{9} paTuTxhiDidu -- aDagisu; adumihAku; damanamADu; hosaki hAku:
\eng{wear down opposition} viroVdhavanunx, parxtiBaTneyanunx
aDagisu, damanamADu.

\num{11} (haDagina \vi) bAvuT hArisu. 
\num{12} (\sA\ niVru \mo vugaLa \vi) savesi, koredu (tUtu, kAluve, \mo
vanunx) mADu; koredu hAku.}}

 \alnum{a} samedu hoVgu; teVyu; jiVNRvAgu; kaqshavAgu; kaSxyisu:
\eng{the stick has worn down to a stump} koVlu samedu hoVgi
moVTAgide. \eng{trousers have been worn out} SarAyi (baLakeyiMda)
jiVNRvAgide. 

 \alnum{b} samedu, aLisi, ujijx -- hoVgu: \eng{the inscription has worn
 away} shAsana samedu hoVgide. \eng{the impression soon wore off} A
aBipArxya beVga aLidu hoVyitu. 
\num{2} baLalihoVgu; daNi, susAtxgu. 
\num{3} bALu; bALike baru; sadayxda sithxtiyalilx yA kAyARcaraNe mADutAtx nidiRSaTx avadhiyavarege uLidiru.
\num{4} (kAlda \vi) nidhAnavAgi -- sari, sAgu, kaLe.}}
 
\noindent

\num{3} \eng{wear (one's years) well} (\AmA) vayasAsxgidadxrU yuvakanAgiyeV kANu.
\num{4} \eng{wear one's \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{heart nuga(34)}{heart} upon one's sleeve.}

 \alnum{a} inunxmuMde baLasalAgadaSuTx baLasu yA baLasalpxDu. 

 \alnum{b} baLalu yA baLalisu; susAtxgu yA susAtxgisu.

\num{8} \eng{wear the sword} yoVdha yA seYnikanAgiru.

\num{11} \eng{wear thin} (tALemx \mo vugaLa \vi) kaDameyAgalu,
(sabaUbau \mo vugaLa \vi) naMbike keDalu -- pArxraMBavAgu.

\bentry
\word[weather(1)]{weather} 
\pron{vedarf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{havA; havAmAna; vAyuguN; oMdu sathxLadalilx, oMdu kAldalilx
 yAvudeV parxdeVshadalilxruva vAyumaMDalda, vAtAvaraNda parisithxti:
 \eng{favourable weather} anukUlkaravAda have. \eng{seasonable
 weather} hitavAda have. \eng{good weather} oLeLxya, utatxma --
 have. \eng{bad weather} keTTx havA. \eng{cold weather} caLi 
 have. \eng{dull weather} maMkAda, beVsara huTiTxsuva
 havA. \eng{rainy weather} maLeya vAtAvaraN. \eng{windy weather}
 birugALiya havA. \eng{he goes out in all weathers} ellx bageya
 havegaLalUlx avanu horage saMcarisutAtxne.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{above the weather} (vimAnayAna) moVDagaLiMdAce shAMtavAda parxdeVshadalilx.
\num{2} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{clerk(1) pagu(3)}{${}^1$clerk} of the weather.}
\num{3} \eng{keep a (\engit{or} one's) weather eye open} ecacxradiMdiru;
 jAgarUkanAgiru. 
\num{4} \eng{make a good (\engit{or} bad) weather of it} (\nw) birugALiyalilx
cenAnxgi (yA keTTxdAgi)vatiRsu, naDe. 
\num{5} \eng{make heavy weather} (samaseyx, kAyARcaraNe, \mo vugaLa) toMdareyanunx, kaSaTxsAdhayxteyanunx atishayisu; yAvudanenxV Agali tiVra kaSaTxveMdu dUru, goVLADu.
\num{6} \eng{under stress of weather} birugALi \mo vugaLa kAraNdiMda.
\hyperdef{W}{weather(1) pagu(7)}{}
\num{7} \eng{under the weather} (\AmA) asavxsathxvAgiru; meY sariyillxdiru yA manasusx samAdhAna sithxtiyalilxllxdiru, parxkuSxbadhxvAgiru.}

\bentry
\word[weather(3)]{weather} 
\pron{vedarf} 
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\kanmu\ oNgisalu, hadamADalu, \mo vugaLigAgi) gALibisilugaLige oDuDx.
\num{2} (\sA\ \kaparx dalilx) (baMDegaLanunx, shilegaLanunx gALimaLegaLige oDiDx) baNNxgeDisu yA shithilgoLisu.
\num{3} (haDagina yA adara nAvika taMDada \vi) (BUshira \mo vugaLa) gALiya dikakxnunx -- muTuTx, talupu.
\num{4} birugALi, birumaLegaLanunx taDedukoMDu surakiSxtavAgi baMdu seVru. 
\num{5} (\rUpa) kaSaTx saMkaTgaLanunx dATi surakiSxta sithxtige baru.
\num{6} (maLeniVru \mo vu nugagxdaMte halgegaLanunx, heMcugaLanunx) oMdara meVloMdaraMte keLamuKvAgi hAyisi joVDisu.}}

you for weeks} ninanxnunx nAnu vAragaLagaTTxLe kaMDillx. \eng{I did it
weeks ago} nAnu adanunx kelvu vAragaLa hiMdeyeV mADide.

 \alnum{c} I avadhiyalilx mADida kelsada avadhi: \eng{42-hour week}

\bentry
\word[weigh(1)]{weigh} 
\pron{veV} 
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (takakxDiyalilx yA itara tulAyaMtarxdiMda) tUgu; tUka mADu; tUka kaMDuhiDi.
\num{2} tUka Uhisalu keYgaLalilx tUgu, tUgi noVDu: \eng{weighed his stick in his hands} tananx koVlnunx tananx keYgaLalilx tUgida.
\num{3} (Ayekx mADalu yA nirAkarisalu) aMdAjumADu; tUginoVDu: \eng{weigh the consequences} pariNAmagaLanunx viveVcisu. \eng{weigh the pros and cons} para matutx viroVdhagaLanunx tUginoVDu. \eng{weigh the merits of candidates} aBayxthiRgaLa ahaRtegaLanunx aMdAjumADu.
\num{4} bele yA pArxmuKyxvanunx aMdAjumADu (\akirx\ saha).
\num{5} (oMdu viSaya \mo vanunx inonxMdaroDane) hoVlisu; tUgu 
\num{6} (hesarisiruva tUkakekx) sarisamanAgiru, (takakxDiyalilx) saritUgu (\akirx\ saha).
\num{7} (nidiRSaTx) pArxmuKyx, mahatatxvX hoMdiru.
\num{8} bal, otAtxya yA parxBAva -- biVru (\akirx\ saha). 
\num{9} (nidiRSaTx) tUkavAgiru; tUkakekx samanAgiru: \eng{weighs a
 ton} oMdu Tnf tUkavAgide. \eng{weighs three kilos} mUru
kiloVgaLaSuTx tUgutatxde.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} tUgu; (nidiRSaTx) tUkavAgiru: \eng{weighs light} tUkadalilx
haguravAgide. 
\num{2} pArxmuKyx yA parxBAva yA mahatatxvX hoMdiru: \eng{my plea
 weighed in his favour} nananx vAda avana paravAgi parxBAva biVritu. 
\num{3} BAravAgiru; horeyAgiru: \eng{responsibility weighed upon him}
jvAbAdxri avana meVle horeyAgi kuLititutx. 
\num{4} ecacxrikeyiMda -- AloVcisu, parigaNisu, viveVcisu, viveVcane
mADu: \eng{weigh well before deciding} nidhaRrisuva, tiVmARna mADuva
modalu cenAnxgi AloVcisu.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{weigh against} tiVmARnada yA kAyaRda meVle parxBAva
biVru. 
\num{2} \eng{weigh \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{anchor(1) pagu(7)}{${}^1$anchor}.}
\num{3} \eng{weigh down} BAradiMda -- bagugx, kugugx, jgugx,
iLibiVLu: 

 \alnum{a} \eng{branches weighed down by fruit} haNiNxniMda jgigxruva
reMbegaLu. 

 \alnum{b} BAradiMda -- bagigxsu, jgigxsu, iLibiVLisu: \eng{fruits weigh
 down the branches} haNuNx reMbegaLanunx jgigxsutatxde. 
\num{4} BAravAgiru; horeyAgiru; kugigxsu: \eng{weighed down with cares}
ciMtegaLiMda kugigxhoVgi. 
\num{5} \eng{weigh in} (muSiTxmallxnanunx paMdayxkekx muMce, kudure
savArananunx jiVnina sahita paMdayxda taruvAya) tUka mADu. 
\num{6} \eng{weigh in with} (\AmA) (vAda \mo vanunx) samathaRvAgi
yA dheYyaRvAgi yA AkarxmaNkAriyAgi -- muMdiDu, muMdoDuDx. 
\num{7} \eng{weigh into} (\AmA) shakitxyutavAgi yA hurupiniMda
(deYhikavAda yA mAtina) -- dALi mADu, AkarxmaN naDasu. 
\num{8}\eng{weigh (heavy etc.) on (\engit{or} upon)} BAravAgiru; horeyAgiru;
manasusx kugigxsu; ciMtege, vayxthege kAraNvAgu. 
\num{9} \eng{weigh one's words} mAtugaLanunx tUka mADi mADi baLasu;
padagaLanunx viveVcaneyiMda baLasu. 
\num{10} \eng{weigh out} (kudure savArananunx jiVnusahita
paMdayxkekx muMce) tUka mADu. \num{11} \eng{weigh out} 

 \alnum{a} (rAshiyiMda nidiRSaTx tUkadadxnunx) tUgi tege. 

 \alnum{b} (rAshiyiMda nidiRSaTx tUkadadxnunx) tUgi -- haMcu, vitarisu. 
\num{12} \eng{weigh with} parxmuKavenisu; mahatatxvXdedxMdenisu;
muKyxvAdadedxMdu toVru, parigaNitavAgu: \eng{the point that weighs
 with me} nanage nananx daqSiTxyalilx muKyxvAda aMshaveMdare. 
\num{13} \eng{weigh up} 

 \alnum{a} (\AmA) aMdAju mADu; mwlyx niNRyisu; bele kaTuTx. 

 \alnum{b} (parxtiBAra yA paDitUkadiMda) etutx; meVlkekxbibxsu:
\eng{bucket is weighed up by the mass of iron at the end of the lever}
sanenxgoVlina inonxMdu tudiyalilxna kabibxNda BAradiMda bakiVTu
meVleVLutatxde. \eng{weigh up ship} (\viparx) haDaganunx niVriniMda 
meVletutx.}

\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{

\bentry
\word[well(3)]{well} 
\pron{velf} 
\gl{\kirxvi} (\tara\ \eng{better}, \tama\ \eng{best}).
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} cenAnxgi; sariyAgi; taqpitxkaravAgi; samapaRkavAgi: \eng{the
work is well done} kelsa cenAnxgi Agide.  
\num{2} sariyAgi; sariyAda riVtiyalilx: \eng{well said} sariyAda mAtu;
sariyAgi heVLida mAtu. \eng{you did well to tell me} niVnu nanage
heVLidudx oLeLxyadAyitu. 
\num{3} saMpUNRvAgi; kUlMkaSavAgi; atayxMta ecacxrikeyiMda: \eng{look
well to it} adanunx ecacxrikeyiMda noVDiko. 
\num{4} bahumaTiTxge; kUDida maTiTxge; bahuteVka: \eng{he is well over
retiring age} avanige, bahuteVka nivaqtitxyAguva vayasusx Agide. 
\num{5} pirxVtiyiMda; vishAvxsadiMda; senxVhadiMda: \eng{treated me
well} nananxnunx vishAvxsadiMda noVDikoMDaru. 
\num{6} bahushaH; nijvAgiyU; sulBavAgi; sakAraNvAgi; viveVkadiMda;
ucita riVtiyiMda: \eng{it may well be that you are right} niVnu
heVLuvudu nijvAgiyU sari irabahudu. \eng{cannot very well refuse the
offer} avaru koDutetxVvenunxvudanunx aSuTx sulBavAgi
nirAkarisalAgadu. 
\num{7} utAsxhadiMda; mecucxgeyiMda; parxshaMsAtamxkavAgi: \eng{speak
well of} mecucxgeyiMda nuDi. \eng{the book was well reviewed}
pusatxkavanunx parxshaMsAtamxkavAgi vimashiRsalAgitutx. 
\num{8} yashasivxyAgi; anukUlvAgi: \eng{it turned out well} adu
aMtayxdalilx yashasivxyAyitu, anukUlvAgi mugiyitu. 
\num{9} adaqSaTxdiMda; samayoVcitavAgi; samayakekx takakxMte,
beVkAdaMte: \eng{well met!} adaqSaTxdiMda BeVTiyAde, samayakekx
sariyAgi sikikxde, niVnu sikidudx oLeLxyadAyitu.  
\num{10} lABakaravAgi; parxyoVjnakaravAgi: \eng{did well for
themselves} tamage lABa mADikoMDaru, lABagaLisi koMDaru.  
\num{11} hAyAgi; ArAmavAgi: \eng{we live well here} nAvu ililx
hAyAgidedxVve.  
\num{12} dhArALavAgi; yatheVcaCxvAgi: \eng{the job pays well} kelsa
dhArALavAgi AdAya niVDutatxde.}} 
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{as well}

 \alnum{a} jtege; saha. 

 \alnum{b} anucitavallxda; sariyAda: \eng{we may as well go} (--ra
badalu) nAvu hoVgaleVbahudu.  

 \alnum{c} ucita; oLeLxyadu: \eng{it would be as well to acquire} hAge
koLuLxvudu ucita.  
\num{2} \eng{as well as} jtege; saha: \eng{he gave me clothes as well
as food} avanu nanage baTeTxya jtege AhAravanUnx koTTx. 
\num{3} \eng{come off well} meVlemx paDe; jyashAliyAgu; kiVtiRgaLisu. 
\num{4} \eng{just as well} paravAgillx; ciMte mADabeVkAgillx; viSAda
paDabeVkAgillx. 
\num{5} \eng{well and truly}

 \alnum{a} nisasxMdeVhavAgi; nijvAgi. 

 \alnum{b} pUtiRyAgi; saMpUNRvAgi.
\num{6} \eng{well aware} cenAnxgi aritu, tiLidu: \eng{well aware of
the danger} apAyavanunx cenAnxgi aritiru. 
\num{7} \eng{well away} 

 \alnum{a} sAkaSuTx -- muMduvaredu, parxgati sAdhisi. 

 \alnum{b} (\AmA) gADhaniderxyalilx yA pUtiR pAnamatatxnAgi. 
\num{8}\eng{well begun is half done} cenAnxgi pArxraMBisida kelsa,
adhaR mugiyiteMdeV lekakx; sariyAgi pArxraMBisidare adhaR mugisidaMte,
sAdhisidaMteyeV. 
\num{9} \eng{well done!} (\eng{\engit{or} well run!}) (parxshaMseya mAtu)
shABAsf! Bale, Bale!  
\num{10} \eng{well out of it} (\eng{\engit{or} well rid of them})
(adaqSaTxvashAtf) hAniyillxde, naSaTxvillxde, toMdareyillxde --
pArAgu: \eng{you are well out of it} sadayx, adaqSaTxvashAtf adariMda
pArAdeyalAlx!  
\num{11} \eng{well with (person)} (obabxna) parxshaMse, mecucxge paDe. 
\num{12} \eng{wish (person) well} (vayxkitxge) shuBa koVru; jyavAgali enunx.}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[well(4)]{well} 
\pron{velf} 
\gl{\gu} (\sA\ \Agu) (\tara\ \eng{better}, \tama\ \eng{best}).
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} AroVgayxda; keSxVmada: \eng{is she well or ill?} avaLu AroVgayxvAgiruvaLoV illxvoV?
\num{2} taqpitxkara; utatxma: \eng{all is well} ellxvU utatxma sithxtiyalilxve.
\num{3} AroVgayxkaravAda: \eng{a well man} AroVgayxvaMta.
\num{4} sUkatxvAda; yukatx; ucitavAda: \eng{it would be well to enquire} vicArisuvudu sUkatx.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{all(2) nuga(4)}{${}^2$all} very well.}
\num{2} \eng{let (\engit{or} leave) well alone} anagatayxvAgi adara
taMTege hoVgabAradu; adaraSaTxkekx adirali. 
\num{3} \eng{well and good} (niNRya \mo vanunx opipxkoLuLxvalilx)
Agabahudu; sariye! \eng{if you choose to take my advice, well and
good} niVnu nananx mAtu keVLuvudAdare, sariye!. 
\num{4} \eng{well enough} sAkaSuTx cenAnxgi, AkaSaRkavAgi.
\num{5} \eng{well off} anukUl sithxtiya; sithxtivaMta; bahuteVka
haNvaMtanAda.}
\eentry

\bentry

\gl{\BAavayx} 
{\dictmeaning{(AshacxyaR, hatAshe, otAtxya, \mo vanunx sUcisuva yA
mAtanADutitxruvAga savxlpx nililxsi taruvAya matetx adanunx

sithxtiyalilx) sari, adanunx biTuTx beVre gatiyeV illx!  
\num{3} \eng{well, but what about Jones?} (tAtAkxlikavAgi oMdu
mAtanunx opipxkoMDu) adeVnoV irabahudu. Adare joVnfsxna viSaya Enu?  
\num{4} \eng{well, here we are at last} (samAdhAna sUcisuvalilx)
abAbx! konegU baMdu seVridevalAlx!

\num{8} \eng{well, who would have thought of it?} (atayxMta AshacxyaR
sUcisuvalilx) are! adu yArige tAneV gotitxtutx?}

\bentry
\word[what(1)]{what} 
\pron{vATf} 
\gl{parxshAnxthaRka \gu} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} yAva; eMtha; eSuTx; Enu: 

 \alnum{a} (anidiRSaTx saMKeyxyiMda AyuvAga \eng{what} padavU,
nidiRSaTx saMKeyxyiMda AyuvAga \eng{which} padavU baLakeyalilxde):
\eng{what books have you read?} niVnu yAva pusatxkagaLanunx
OdididxVye? \eng{don't know what plan he will try} avanu yAva upAya
baLasutAtxnoV tiLiyadu. 

 \alnum{b} (\AmA) \eng{= \hyperlink{which(1)}{which}: what book have you
chosen} niVnu yAva pusatxka ArisididxVye? 

 \alnum{c} (vasutxgaLa motatx, saMKeyx,
vivaraNe beVkeMdukoLuLxvalilx): \eng{what men, abilities, has he?}
avana baLi eMtha jnaru, yAva yoVgayxte -- sAmathaRyxgaLu, ive? 
\num{2} (AshacxyaRsUcaka \gu) eSuTx; eMtha (mahatatx vxdudx,
vicitarxvAdadudx yA asAdhAraNvAdadudx enunxvalilx): \eng{what a fool
 you are?} niVnu eMtha aviveVki? \eng{what impudence} eMtha, eSuTx
-- dhASaTxRyx?  \eng{what partial judges we are?} nAveMthA
pakaSxpAtadaqSiTxya nAyxyAdhiVsharu? 
\hypertarget{what(1)3}{}
\num{3} (saMbaMdhasUcaka \gu) yAva; eMtha; eSuTx: \eng{lend me what
 money you can} ninageSuTx sAdhayxvoV aSuTx haN nanage sAl koTiTxru.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{what good \engit{or} use is it} adariMda yAva parxyoVjna, yAva oLitu? 
\num{2} \eng{what matter?} adariMda EnAgabeVku? (`EnAdarU ciMteyillx' eMbathaRdalilx).}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[what(2)]{what} 
\pron{vATf} 
\gl{\sanA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (parxshAnxthaRka savaRnAmavAgi) Enu; eSuTx; yAva: \eng{what
 is your name?} ninanx hesareVnu? \eng{don't know what she said}
avaLu Enu heVLidaLoV tiLiyadu. 
\num{2} (parxshenxgaLu niSeVdhAthaRka heVLikegaLa rUpadalilx):
\eng{what is the use of trying?} parxyatinxsi tAneV Enu parxyoVjna? 
\num{3} (kelvomemx inonxbabxna mAtu sariyAgi keVLisade, athaRvAgade,
iruvAga, matotxmemx parxshenx, sapxSaTxne, keVLuvalilx): \eng{what?
 you did what?} Enu? niVnu Enu mADide aMta heVLide? \eng{what, do you
 really mean it?} EnaMde? nijvAgi, adu ninanx iMgitaveV? (\AmA)
\eng{nice day, what?} sogasAda dina! EnaMtiVye? 
\num{4} (AshacxyaRsUcaka \sanA): eSoTxMdu!: \eng{what he must have
 suffered} avanu eSoTxMdu (saMkaT) anuBavisirabeVku! 
\hypertarget{what(2)5}{} \hypertarget{what2 pagu5}{}
\num{5} (saMbaMdhasUcaka \sanA) (yAvudoV) adu yA avu: \eng{what
 followed was unpleasant} muMdeVnAyiteMbaudu bahaLa
ahitakaravAgitutx. \eng{what I have written I have written} nAnu Enu
baredidedxVnoV, baredidedxVne, aSeTx. \eng{it is the poor what gets 
 the blame} (\ashi) keTTx hesaru baruvudu baDavarige mAtarx.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{come what may} EneV barali; baMdadudx barali. 
\num{2}\eng{I know (\engit{or} you know what he is \engit{or} what it is)} adeVnu
(yA avanu eMthavanu) eMbaudu nanage yA ninage gotutx. 
\num{3} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_k.pdf}{K}{know(1) nuga(28)}{${}^1$know} what's what.} 
\num{4} \eng{\engit{or} what} heVge; athavA inenxVnu (beVre Enu?): \eng{are
 you trying to kill me, or what?} niVnu nananxnunx
kollxleLesutitxdidxVyoV, heVge? 
\num{5} \eng{so what?} 

 \alnum{a} AdareVnaMte?: \eng{he hates me; so what?} avanu nananxnunx
devxVSisutAtxne; AdareVnaMte? adu sadayxkekx parxsakatxvallx. 

 \alnum{b} adakekx parihAravillx, beVre upAyavillx,
mAgaRvillx. \eng{tell you what (\engit{or} I will tell you what)} nAnu heVLetxVne keVLu .... (nananx mAtu keVLililx). 
\num{6} \eng{what then?} muMdeVnAgabahudu (idariMda muMdeVnu
pariNAmavAgabahudu?) 
\num{7} \eng{what about?} EkAgabAradu? Enu samAcAra? idakekx
EnaMtiVye? ninanx aBipArxyaveVnu? nAnu heVLuvudu EneMdare.... :
\eng{what about a game of chess} Iga oMdu AT caduraMga Eke ADabAradu?
\eng{what-d' you (\engit{or} what d'ye)-call-it (etc.) (\engit{or} what's-its)
 (\engit{or} his)-name (\engit{or} is it, what you may call it)} adeVnoV adara
hesaru EnoV heVLAtxralAlx ... Acnx adeV ... adara hesaru ... EnoV
aMdare ... itAyxdi. 
\num{8} \eng{what do you say} (\ame\ \eng{what say)} (\AmA) nananx
salhe EneMdare ... : \eng{what do you say we have a rest} nananx
salhe 
EneMdare nAvu vishArxMti paDeyoVN. 
\num{9} \eng{what will people say?} jna EnaMdukoMDAru! (`idu
gwravAhaRvallx' eMbathaRdalilx). 
\num{10} \eng{what for?} Eke? EtakAkxgi? EtakokxVsakxra? 
\num{11} \eng{what have you} ninanx baLi (aMthadeV inUnx) EneVnide
... EnelAlx ive ... 
\num{12} \eng{what ho!} (dUradiMda yAranAnxdarU kUgi kareyuva
udAgxradalilx yA saMdhisidAga heVLuva mAtu): `Oyf ... yAralilx?'
`yArididxVri, alilx?' EnirxV. 
\num{13} \eng{what if} `AdareVnaMte?' 
\num{14} \eng{what is he?} avana vaqtitx Enu? avanu yAva kelsadalilx
(nwkariyalilx) idAdxne? avana aMtasetxVnu? avanu eMthavanu? (itAyxdi). 
\num{15} \eng{what is it like?} adu heVgide (adara savxrUpa Enu?) 
\num{16} \eng{what is more} (jotege visheVSavAgi EnanAnxdarU seVrisi
heVLuvAga): aSuTx mAtarxvallx, mAtarxvallxde. 
\num{17} \eng{what next?} (idakikxMta hecucx aviveVkavAdudu,
dhASaRTxyXvAdudu yA vilkaSxNvAdudu yA hosadAdudu Enide?
eMbathaRdalilx) muMdeVnu? hAgAdare -- AmeVle, muMde? 
\num{18} \eng{what not} (aneVka vasutx \mo vanunx paTiTx mADi
heVLuvAga) `inUnx iMtha hatutx halvu'; inUnx EneVnoV: \eng{sheets,
 napkins and what not} hodeyuva magagxluhAsigegaLu, keYcwkagaLu
inUnx EneVnoV. 
\num{19} \eng{what of} (adara/avana/avara/kurita) sudidx Enu,
samAcAraveVnu? 
\num{20} \eng{what of it?} = \hyperlink{what2 pagu5}{\pagu\ $(5)$}. 
\num{21} \eng{what \hyperref{kandict_t.pdf}{T}{though(1) pagu(2)}{${}^1$though}.}}} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word{wheedle} 
\pron{viVDa(Df)lf} 
\gl{\sakirx} 
\dictmeaning{

vugaLiMda) maruLu mADu; olisu; pusalAyisu; beNeNxhacucx; tale savaru:
\eng{she wheedled him into going to the theatre with her} (\AmA)
tananx jate nATkamaMdirakekx hoVguvaMte avaLu avananunx pusalAyisidaLu. 
\num{2} pusalAyisi, olisi (vayxkitx \mo variMda) EnanAnxdarU --
kasiduko, kitutxko, vasUlumADu, piVkisu, giTiTxsu: \eng{she wheedled
 a new car out of her father} avaLu avaLapapxnanunx olisi hosa kAru
piVkisidaLu. 
\num{3} (vayxkitx \mo varanunx) pusalAyisi moVsa mADu.}

\bentry

\gl{\nA}

hatoVTiyalilxDutAtx; niyaMtirxsutAtx.

\num{3} \eng{break on the wheel} (shikiSxsabeVkAdavaranunx madhayxyugadalilx mADutitxdadx hAge) daMDana cakarxkekx kaTiTx citarxhiMse mADu, kolulx.
\num{4} \eng{go on (\engit{or} oiled) wheels} sullitavAgi hoVgu, calisu.

\num{6} \eng{put a \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{spoke(1) pagu}{${}^1$spoke} in (person's) wheel.}

AjAcnxshabadxvAgi) balkekx (yA eDakekx) daMDavaqtatxvAgi tirugi. 
\num{8} \eng{wheel of life}

 \alnum{a} \eng{= \hyperref{kandict_z.pdf}{Z}{zoetrope}{zoetrope}.} 

 \alnum{b} (bwdadhxdhamaRdalilx heVLuva) (vayxkitxya) jnamxcakarx;
niraMtara jnAmxMtara cakarxgaLu.

jiVvanacakarxgaLu.

 \alnum{a} sUkaSx mx jTil yaMtarx.

avugaLige saMbaMdhisidaMte; yAvudeV sathxLakekx, kaDege, dikikxge:
\eng{go where you like} iSaTx baMda kaDege hoVgu. \eng{that is where
 you are wrong} niVnu tapupx mADiruvudu alilxyeV. \eng{delete where
 not applicable} anavxyisadiruva kaDe hoDeduhAku. 
\num{2} matutx alilx: \eng{reached Mandya, where the car broke down} 
maMDayxkekx talupidevu, alilx kAru keTuTxhoVyitu.}

\bentry
\word[while(1)]{while} 
\pron{veYlf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (kelsa \mo vakekx hiDida, viniyoVgisida, kaLeda) hotutx;
veVLe; samaya; avadhi; kAl: \eng{go away for a while} savxlpx hotutx
horaTuhoVgu. 
\num{2} 
\alnum{a} beVroMdu kirxyeya, kelsada madheyx, naDuve. 

 \alnum{b} (\kAparx) Aga; A hotutx; A samayada -- madheyx, naDuve.
\num{3} savxlpx kAl, samaya: \eng{have not seen you a while}
savxlpxkAldiMda ninanxnunx noVDillx.}} 
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{a good (\engit{or} great) while} bahaLa kAl; sumAru hotutx.
\num{2} \eng{all the while} A iDiV samayadalilx; udadxkUkx.
\num{3} \eng{between whiles} (beVre, itara kelsagaLu, GaTnegaLu, \mo vugaLa) naDuve. 
\num{4} \eng{for a long while} bahaLa kAldiMda: \eng{have not seen
 him for a long while} bahaLa kAldiMdalU avananunx noVDillx. 
\num{5} \eng{(for) a while} savxlpx kAldiMda. 
\num{6} \eng{in a (\engit{or} little) while} beVgane; koMca, savxlpx
-- hotitxnalilx. 
\num{7} \eng{once in a while} AgaloV IgaloV omemx; yAvAgalAdaromemx. 
\eng{he will make it worth your while} ninage takakxSuTx
parxtiPal koDutAtxne. 
\num{8} \eng{the while (\engit{or} whilst)} 

 \alnum{a} (\kAparx) Aga; A hotutx; A veVLe. 

 \alnum{b} beVre kelsada samayadalilx.
\hypertarget{while(1) pagu(9)}{}
\num{9} \eng{worth one's while} parxyoVjnakAriyAda; upayukatx;
sAthaRka: \eng{it isn't worth while going there} alilxge
hoVguvudariMda EnU parxyoVjnavillx.} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word[while(3)]{while} 
\pron{veYlf} 
\gl{\saMavayx}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} Aga; adeV samayakekx (sariyAgi); adeV kAldalilx: \eng{please
 write while I dictate} nAnu heVLuvAga niVnu dayaviTuTx bareduko. 
\num{2} Adare; AdarU; AdAgUyx: \eng{Nero was fiddling while Rome was
 burning} roVmf nagara hotitx uriyutitxdadxrU, niVroV (cakarxvatiR)
piTiVlu bArisutitxdadx. \eng{while convinced it is true, I cannot
 prove it} adu satayxveMdu nanage manavarikeyAgidAdxgUyx, adanunx
rujuvAtu mADalAre. 
\num{3} (\kanu\ iMgelxMDf \parx)varegU: \eng{wait while Monday}
soVmavAradavaregU kAyu.} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word[whip(1)]{whip} 
\pron{vipf} 
\gl{\sakirx} (\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{whipped}; \vakaq\ \eng{whipping}).
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} taTkakxne, Pakakxne -- calisu, tegeduko, kiVLu, hiri, kasiduko,
hoDe, nugugx, horaDu (\akirx\ saha): \eng{whip out a sword}
sarakakxne katitx hiri. \eng{whip away the tablecloth} meVjina
musukanunx pakakxne eLedu hAku. \eng{whip off your coat} taTkakxne
ninanx koVTnunx kaLacu, kitetxse. 
\num{2} (huri, koVlu, \mo vakekx) hatatxnAgi dAra sututx. 
\num{3} cAvaTiyiMda -- hoDe, bArisu, tiVDu. 
\num{4} cAvaTiyiMda hoDedu -- naDesu, ODisu, oTuTx seVrisu. 
\num{5} balvAgi dUSisu, tegaLu.
\num{6} (moTeTx, hAlina kene, \mo vanunx) (noregaTuTxvaMte) goTAyisu;
kaDe; tiVDu. 
\num{7} (\birx) (\ashi) kadi; lpaTAyisu: \eng{who has whipped my
 pen?} yAru nananx penanxnunx kadadxvaru? 
\num{8} (\ashi) 

 \alnum{a} miVru; miVrisu. 

 \alnum{b} soVlisu.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{whip in} (beVTenAyigaLanunx) (cAvaTiyiMda) oTuTxgUDisu,
oTiTxge seVrisu. 
\num{2} \eng{whip off = \hyperlink{whip(1)}{${}^1$whip(1)}.}
\num{3} \eng{whip on} kelsakekx toDagisu; kAyaRkekx perxVrisu.
\num{4} \eng{whip up}

 \alnum{a} (BAvane \mo vanunx) keraLisu; parxcoVdisu. 

 \alnum{b} (hAjrAgalu) kare niVDu; AdeVshisu.}

\num{2} beVTegArana sahAyaka; beVTenAyigaLu cedaradaMte maMde hoDeyuva, beVTe sahAyaka.
\num{3} (shAsanasaBe \mo vugaLalilx) 

 \alnum{a} shisutxpAlka; pAliRmeMTinalilx oMdu pakaSxda sadasayxra
shisutx noVDikoLuLxvudu, avaru saBegaLige baruvaMte noVDikoLuLxvudu,
avarige beVkAda tiLivaLikeyanunx koDuvudu, \mo\ kAyaRkAkxgi
neVmitanAdavanu.

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} siLuLx -- hAku, hoDe; siVTi Udu; shiLeLx
 hAku.
\num{2} (saMkeVta niVDalu yA AshacxyaR yA tirasAkxra sUcisalu)
 siLeLx hAku; siLeLx hAki -- saMkeVta koDu, AshacxyaR yA tirasAkxra
 sUcisu.
\num{3} (hakikx) siLiLxna shabadxmADu.
\num{4} (kiSxpaNi,
 gALi, \mo vu) siLuLxsadidxnoDane royayxne calisu.
\num{5} (nAyi \mo
 vanunx) kareyalu siLuLxhAku.}} 
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{let (person) go whistle} 

 \alnum{a} (obabxna Ase, apeVkeSxgaLanunx) upeVkiSxsu; kaDegaNisu; lekikxsadiru:
 \eng{he said we could go whistle for our money} namamx haNkAkxgi
 siLuLx hAkutatx kUruvaMte avanu heVLida (aMdare
 kaDegaNisida). 

 \alnum{b} (obabxna mAtu \mo vugaLa virudadhx)
 tirasAkxradiMda -- nagu, AshacxyaR sUcisu. 
\num{2} \eng{whistle down
 the wind} 

 \alnum{a} (DeVge beVTe) DeVgeyanunx (hAralu) biDu;
 hArihoVguvaMte biDu. 

 \alnum{b} keYbiDu; tore; biTuTxbiDu;
 tayxjisu.
\num{3} \eng{whistle for} (\AmA) vayxthaRvAgi -- haMbalisu,
 bAyibAyi biDu; hapahapisu.
\num{4} \eng{whistle for a wind}
 (nivARta sathxLadalilx sikikxkoMDa nAvikaru) gALigAgi -- siLuLxhAku,
 haMbalisu.
\num{5} \eng{whistle in the dark} katatxllilx
 siLeLxhAku; hedarillxveMbaMte naTisu; Bayavanunx, BiVtiyanunx --
 gelulx, jyisu. 
\num{6} \eng{whistle up} (nAyi, seVvaka, \mo vanunx)
 siLeLx hAki, Udi -- kare, baruvaMte heVLu.}

\bentry

 \eng{white as a sheet} (shava) vasatxrXdaMte biLicikoMDa. 
\num{3}
 (jiVvaveYjAcnxnika kAraNgaLiMda) huTuTxvAgaleV biLicikoMDiruva;
 (deVha, camaR, kUdalu, \mo vugaLu) huTiTxniMdaleV beLaLxgAgiruva;
 AjnamxshevxVta: \eng{white mouse} (huTuTxvAgaleV) biLicikoMDiruva
 ili. 
\num{4} (adeV vagaRda uLidavugaLigiMta) kaDame
 kapapxgiruva. 
\num{5} 
\alnum{a} (kUdalina \vi) (\kanmu\
 vayoVdhamaRdiMda) beLaLxgAda; nareta. 

 \alnum{b} (vayxkitxya \vi)
 biLigUdalina; naregUdalina; kUdalu naretiruva. 
\num{6} nasubiLupina;
 biLipu seVrida; koMca biLupAda. 
\num{7} 
\alnum{a} (sasayxda \vi)
 biLi hU yA haNuNx biDuva: \eng{white cauliflower} biLi
 hUkoVsu. 

 \alnum{b} (marada \vi) biLi togaTeya: \eng{white ash}
 biLi AYxSf mara.
\num{8} (niVru, gALi, gAju, \mo vugaLa \vi) biLi;
 baNNxvillxda; vaNRrahita; nivaRNR; pAradashaRka: \eng{white glass}
 biLigAju. 
\num{9} (\AmA) nimaRl; shuci; sAdhu; niSakxLaMka;
 neYtikavAgi (pari)shudadhx. 
\num{10} \eng{(White)}
 shevxVtavaNiRVyara; biLi jnAMgadavara: \eng{white civilization}
 biLiyara nAgarikate. \eng{white woman} biLiya (jnAMgada)
 heMgasu. 
\num{11} \eng{(White)} (\ca) kArxMtiviroVdhi; parxtigAmi:
 \eng{white army} parxtigAmigaLa seYnayx. 
\num{12} (veYnina \vi)
 biLiya; biLi dArxkiSxyiMda yA sipepx tegeda kari dArxkiSxyiMda
 tayArisida, mADida.

 seVrisiruva.}}

\bentry
\word{who} 
\pron{hU} 
\gl{\sanA} 
{\dictmeaning{(divxtiyA viBakitx
 \eng{whom} \ucAcx\ hUmf yA \AmA \eng{who} \ucAcx\ hU;
 SaSiThxVviBakitx \eng{whose} \ucAcx\ hUsfZ).
\num{1} (parxshAnxthaRka) 

 \alnum{a} yAru? yAvanu? yAvaLu?: \eng{who said
 so?} hAge heVLidavaru yAru? \eng{who would have thought of it?}
 (yArU adanunx yoVcisutitxralillx eMba athaRdalilx) yAru
 tAneV adanunx yoVcisutitxdadxru? \eng{whom \engit{or} who did you see?}
 niVnu yAranunx noVDide? 

 \alnum{b} yAru? eMthavanu? eMthavaLu?
 eMthavaru?: \eng{who am I to object?} AkeSxVpisalu nAnu yAru?
 (nanageVnu hakukx?)
\num{2} (niSeVdhasUcaka parxshenxyAgi) \eng{who
 would have thought of it?} hAgeMdu yAru tAneV
 yoVcisidadxru?
\num{3} A (vayxkitx); aMtha vayxkitx: \eng{any one who
 wishes can come} yAru baralu iciPxsutAtxroV avaru
 barabahudu. \eng{the woman who you met?} niVnu BeVTimADida
 heMgasu. \eng{the man who you saw} niVnu noVDida vayxkitx (koneya
 eraDu udAharaNegaLalilx \eng{whom} sariyAda parxyoVga, Adare
 sAmAnayx saMdaBaRgaLalilx \eng{who} eMdu parxyoVga).
\num{4} matutx
 yA Adare avanu, avaLu, avaru, \mo: \eng{sent it to Ram, who gave it
 to Lakshman} adanunx rAmanige kaLuhisida, matutx (yA Adare) avanu
 adanunx lkaSx mxNnige koTTx.
\num{5} (\pArxparx) yAru; yAreV Agali;
 yAvudeV vayxkitx; yAvanu(Lu): \eng{who steals my purse steals
 trash} yAru nananx ` pasaR' nunx kadiyuvaroV avaru
 kelsakekx bAradadxnunx kadadxhAge lekakx (yArAdarU nananx haN
 kadadxre nanageVnU naSaTxvillx eMbathaRdalilx). \eng{whom the gods
 love die young} yAra meVle deVvara kaqpe ideyoV aMthavaru cikakx
 vayasisxnalelxV (beVga) sAyutAtxre.}} 
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{as who should say} hAgeMdu
 heVLidavana riVtiyalilx; yAroV hAge heVLidareMbaMte. 
\num{2}
 \eng{who-does-what dispute \engit{or} strike} (jgaLa, vivAda, saMpu, \mo
 vugaLa \vi) yAru yAvudanunx mADabeVku enunxvudu; yAra kelsa Enu
 enunxvudu.
\num{3} \eng{who goes there? = \hyperref{kandict_g.pdf}{G}{gopagu67}{go}} (\pagu\ \eng{67}).
\num{4}\eng{who is it} (hesaru nenapAgadiruvAga) adu yAroV
 obabxru.}

\bentry
\word[whole(1)]{whole} 
\pron{hoVlf} 
\gl{\gu} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (\pArxparx) AroVgayxvAgiruva; susithxtiyalilxruva;
 savxsathx: \eng{thy faith hath made thee whole} ninanx naMbike
 ninanxnunx susithxtiyaliTiTxde.
\num{2} susithxtiyalilxruva;
 hAnigoLagAgada; apAyakekx tutAtxgada: \eng{hope you will be back
 whole} susithxtiyalilx, nirapAyavAgi hiMtirugi barutitxVyeMdu
 niriVkiSxsutetxVne. 
\num{3} pUNR; Binanxvallxda.
\num{4} iDiV;
 pUtiR; saMpUNRvAda; aKMDavAda; samagarxvAda: \eng{swallowed it
 whole} adanunx iDiyAgi nuMgida. \eng{tell the whole truth}
 pUtiR nij heVLu. \eng{the whole school knows} iDiV shAlegeV
 gotutx.
\num{5} savaR; samasatx; ellx; saMpUNR: \eng{the whole
 priesthood} saMpUNR puroVhitavagaR; ellx puroVhitaru.
\num{6}
 (rakatx, hAlu, \mo vugaLa \vi) yAvudeV aMsha tegedu hAkirada,
 beVpaRDisirada: \eng{whole milk} (kobaubx, kene, \mo vanunx
 tegeyada) shudadhx hAlu.}} 
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{bread made of whole meal} tavuDu
 tegeyada hiTiTxna berxDuDx.
\num{2} \eng{do thing with (one's) whole
 heart} manasAre, manaHpUNaRvAgi -- kelsa mADu.
\num{3} \eng{got off
 with a whole skin} EnoMdU apAyavillxde tapipxsikoMDa.
\num{4}
 \eng{go (the) whole \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{hog(1) nuga(1)}{${}^1$hog}.}
\num{5} \eng{out of whole cloth} (\ame)
 suLuLx; saMpUNaRvAgi saqSaTxne mADida; suLuLx saqSiTxya.}

 tiLiyadu.
\num{2} (adhAyxhAra \parx dalilx) Eke?: \eng{you are late,
 why ?} niVnu taDavAgi baMdiruve, Eke?
\num{3} (saMbaMdhasUcaka \kirxvi) yAva kAraNgaLigoVsakxra?; Eke? yAvudakAkxgi?: \eng{the
 reasons why he did it are obscure} avanu adanunx mADidadxkekx
 kAraNgaLeVnoV tiLiyadu; avanu EtakokxVsakxra hAge mADidanoV
 tiLiyadu.}}

\bentry
%\hyperdef{W}{will(1)}{}
\word[will(1)]{will} 
\pron{vilf}
sahAyaka
\gl{\kirx}
{\dictmeaning{(utatxmapuruSa, madhayxma puruSa, taqtiVya puruSa, \Eva\
 vataRmAna \eng{will}; madhayxma puruSa, \Eva\ vataRmAna
 pArxparx. \eng{wilt} \ucAcx\ vilfTx; \BU\ matutx \BUkaq\
 \eng{would} \ucAcx\ vuDf). (heVLike, Ajecnx yA parxshenxgaLalilx)
 BaviSayxkAl sUcaka: \eng{you will regret this} niVnidakekx
 viSAdapaDutitxVye. \eng{you will leave at once} niVnu kUDaleV
 horaTuhoVga beVku. \eng{will you come} niVnu barutitxVyA?
\num{1} bayasu; Ashisu; udedxVshisu; iciPxsu: (\pArxparx) \eng{what wilt
 thou?} ninage Enu beVku? \eng{what would they?} avaru Enu
 iciCxsuvaru?
\num{2} (iceCx, opipxge yA olvugaLanunx) sUcisu; Ashisu;
 AsepaDu; beVkAgu: \eng{come when you will} ninage yAvAga beVkoV, Aga
 bA.
\num{3} opupx; samamxtisu: \eng{would not go any further}
 (idakikxMta inUnx) hecucx muMduvariyalu opepxnu.
\num{4} rUDhiya,
 aBAyxsa yA anivAyaR parxvaqtitxyanunx sUcisu: \eng{will sit there
 for hours} gaMTegaTTxle alilx kuLitukoLuLxtAtxne. \eng{accidents
 will happen} apaGAtagaLu saMBavisutatxve, AgiyeV Agutatxve,
 naDadeV naDeyutatxve.
\num{5} (utatxmapuruSadalilx) (nidhARra,
 udedxVsha, iceCx, \mo vanunx) sUcisu: \eng{I will not be caught
 again} nAnu matetx sikikxbiVLuvudillx. \eng{I will return soon}
 nAnu beVga vApasAgutetxVne.
\num{6} shakitx, sAmathaRyx sUcisu:
 \eng{the jar will hold a kilo} jADi oMdu kiloV hiDisutatxde. \eng{I
 will manage it} nAnu adanunx nivaRhisabalelx
 (nivaRhisutetxVne).
\num{7} saMBava yA niriVkeSxyanunx sUcisu: \eng{that
 will be my wife} avaLu nananx heMDati AgutAtxLe (Aguva
 saMBavavide).
\num{8} (\AmA) \eng{= \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{shall(5)}{shall(5)}:
 I would like to disagree} nAnu opapxliciPxsuvudillx.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1}\eng{I wouldn't know} (niriVkiSxsuva hAge)
 nanage tiLiyadu; nanage gotitxllx.
\num{2} \eng{will do} (\AmA)

\alnum{a} (koVrikeyanunx neraveVrisuva mAtAgi) Agali; hAge
 mADutetxVne. \eng{we would have come if you had told us} niVnu
 modaleV heVLidadxre nAvu barutitxdedxvu. 

\alnum{b} \eng{that will \hyperref{kandict_d.pdf}{D}{do(1) nuga(34)}{${}^1$do}} (\pagu\ $34$).
\num{3} \eng{would God} deVvaru mADisidadxre,
 karuNisidadxre: \eng{would God that I were dead} nAnu sAyuvaMte
 deVvaru anugarxhisidadxre cenAnxgitutx!
\num{4} \eng{would I were}
 iceCxpaDuve; Ashisuve: \eng{would I were a bird} nAnoMdu
 hakikxyAgidadxre (cenAnxgitutx).} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word[will(2)]{will} 
\pron{vilf} 
\gl{\nA}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} iSaTx; iceCx; irAde; udedxVsha; saMkalpx;
 nidhARra: \eng{the mind consists of the understanding and the will}
 manasusx eMbaudaralilx jAcnxna matutx saMkalpx (eraDU)
 seVrive.
\num{2} parxbal Ase; daqDha AkAMkeSx: \eng{the patient's will
 to live is the surgeon's best ally} roVgige tAnu badukaleVbeVkeMba
 parxbal Ase iruvudu, shasatxrXveYdayxnige bahaLaSuTx
 oLeLxyadu.
\num{3} daqDha nidhARra; saMkalpxbal; savxMta
 iceCxgaLanunx neraveVrisikoLuLxva, inonxbabxra meVle
 saMpUNR hatoVTi sAdhisuva shakitx: \eng{with a will} daqDha
 nidhARradiMda, saMkalpxdiMda. 
\num{4} (\pArxparx) vayxkitxya -- niriVkeSxgaLu, iSATxniSaTxgaLu, Ase
 AkAMkeSxgaLu: \eng{thy will be done} ninanx iSaTxdaMteyeV Agali; ninanx
 iSaTxveV neraveVrali! 
\num{5}
 (savxMta) viveVcane; yukAtxyukatx jAcnxna. 
\num{6} (inonxbabxra
 bagegx) olvu; manasusx; manoVvaqtitx; iSaTx: \eng{good will}
 sadudedxVsha; pirxVti. \eng{ill will} durudedxVsha; devxVSa.
\num{7}
 (\sA\ liKita) uyilu; aMtima iSaTxpatarx; maraNshAsana; tananx
 Asitxyanunx tananx maraNAnaMtara heVge haMcabeVkenunxvudanunx
 tiLisiruva kAnUnubadadhxvAda (\sA\ liKita) sUcanegaLu: \eng{make
 one's will} uyilu mADu, barediDu.
\num{8} = \eng{\hyperlink{will-power}{will-power}}.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{at will}

  \alnum{a} iSATxnusAra;
 iceCxyaMte. 

 \alnum{b} (\nAyxshA) icACxnusAra; yAva sUcaneyanUnx
 koDade horahAkabahudAda, KAlimADisabahudAda: \eng{tenant at will}
 icACxnusArada bADigedAra; iSaTxbaMdAga biDisabahudAda bADigedAra yA
 hiDuvaLidAra.
\num{2} \eng{a will of one's own} (\sw) moMDutana;
 haTmAritana; Cal.
\num{3} \eng{freedom of the will} = \hyperlink{will pagu4}{\pagu ($4$).}
\hypertarget{will pagu4}{}
\num{4}\eng{free will} saMkalpx, icACx -- sAvxtaMtarxyx;
 savxtaMtarx saMkalpx shakitx: \eng{did it of my own free will}
 nananx savxtaMtarx saMkalpxshakitxyiMdaleV nAnu adanunx
 mADide.
\num{5} \eng{have one's will} tanage beVkAdudu sikukxvaMte
 mADiko; tananx iceCxyaMte mADisiko.
\num{6} \eng{last will and
 testament} uyilu; maraNshAsana.
\num{7} \eng{what is your will ?}
 Enu mADabeVkenunxve?
\num{8} \eng{where there's a will there's a
 way} manasisxdadxre mAgaR(virutatxde); saMkalpxvidedxDe
 dAriyirutatxde (aDacaNegaLanunx dATbahudu).
\num{9} \eng{with the
 best will in the world} obabxna udedxVsha eSeTxV
 udAtatxvAgidadxrU.}

\bentry
\word[win(1)]{win} 
\pron{vinf}
\gl{\sakirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (hoVrAT, jUju,
 sapxdheR, vAyxjyx, parxyatanx, \mo vugaLiMda) gelulx; gaLisu; paDe;
 sAdhisiko: \eng{won some money} savxlpx haN gaLisida. \eng{won my
 admiration} nananx mecucxge paDeda.
\num{2} (yudadhx, kirxVDe,
 paMdayx, \mo vugaLalilx) gelulx; jyisu; gaLisu; yashasusx paDe:
 \eng{win the battle} kadana gelulx. \eng{win a prize} bahumAna
 gelulx.
\num{3} (gaNiyiMda) aduru -- tege, paDe.
\num{4}
 parxyatanxdiMda -- hoVgi seVru, talpu, muTuTx: \eng{win the shore}
 daDa seVru. \eng{win the summit} shiKra talpu.
\num{5} tananx kaDe
 mADiko; olisiko: \eng{he soon won his audience over} bahaLa beVga
 avanu perxVkaSxkaranunx olisikoMDa.
\num{6} (hululx \mo vanunx)
 gALigoDiDx, gALiyalilx haravi -- oNgisu.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (jUju, sapxdheR, \mo vugaLalilx)
 jyashAliyAgu; gelulx: \eng{he applied for a scholarship and won}
 avanu vidAyxthiR veVtanakekx ajiR hAkidudx gedadx. \eng{who won?}
 yAru gedadxru? \eng{persevere, and you will win} biDade
 parxyatanxmADu, niVnu gelulxve.
\num{2} (\AmA) satata
 parxyatanxdiMda muMduvare, sAdhisu, niBAyisu: \eng{he won through
 all difficulties} avanu kaSaTxgaLanenxlAlx niBAyisida.
\num{3}
 (\pArxparx) hecucxhecAcxgi mecucxgege baru: \eng{a theory that wins
 upon one by degrees} (karxmeVN) hecucxhecAcxgi obabxra mecucxge
 gaLisaballx vicAra, vAda, ciMtane.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{win etc. \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{hand(1) nuga(76)}{${}^1$hands} down.}
\num{2}
 \eng{win one's spurs } 

 \alnum{a} (\AmA) yashasusx yA KAyxtiyanunx -- gaLisu,
 paDe. 

 \alnum{b} (\ca) neYTfpadavi paDe.
\num{3} \eng{win one's way}
 hoVrADi sAdhisu; hoVrATdiMda mAgaR mADiko. 
\num{4} \eng{win over}
 olisiko; beMbal, utetxVjna, sahAya -- paDe, gaLisu.
\num{5} \eng{win (person's) confidence} obabxna naMbike, vishAvxsa gaLisu.
\num{6}
 \eng{win the day} (\engit{or}) \pArxparx\ \eng{(field)} yudadhxdalilx
 (rUpakavAgi vAda \mo vugaLalilx) jyashAliyAgu 
\num{7} \eng{win the toss} TAsf gelulx; (soVlu gelvu nidhaRrisuva) nANyxda
 cimumxvikeyalilx gelulx.
\num{8}\eng{win through (\engit{or} out)}
 aDetaDegaLanunx dATu, nivArisiko, jyisu.
\num{9} \eng{you can't win}
 (\AmA) (yAva riVtiyiMdalU) niVnu gellxlu sAdhayxvillx,
 gellxlAre. 
\num{10} \eng{you can't win them all} (\AmA) ellxranUnx
 gellxlu sAdhayxvillx (soVtAga samAdhAna mADikoLuLxva mAtu).}
\eentry

\bentry
\word[wind(1)]{wind} 
\pron{viMDf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} 
\alnum{a} (biVsu)gALi; mAruta; pavana; vAyu; vAta;
 anil; elru: \eng{hot wind} bisigALi; uSaNxvAyu. 

 \alnum{b} (nidiRSaTx dikikxniMda biVLuva yA visheVSa riVtiya) gALi; mAruta:
 \eng{north wind} utatxra mAruta; baDagu gALi. \eng{fair wind}
 (haDagina calnege) anukUlvAda gALi. \eng{contrary wind} parxtikUl
 mAruta; edurugALi. \eng{constant wind} oMdu sathxLadalilx yAvAgalU
 oMdeV dikikxnalilx biVsuva gALi; gotutxgALi; niyata mAruta.
\num{2} gALiya dikukx, kaDe: \eng{take (\engit{or} get) the wind of} (matotxMdu
 haDagige gALi tapipxsuvaMte adara) gALipakakxkekx hoVgu 
\num{3} poLuLxnuDi; ToLuLxmAtu; shabAdxDaMbara.
\num{4} (kaqtakavAgi
 uMTumADida) vAyuparxvAha; parxvAhavAgi baLasalu sheVKrisiTTx vAyu;
 vAyusaMgarxha.
\num{5} 
\alnum{a} (samUhavAcaka) (vAdayxmeVLadalilx)
 gALi, vAyu -- vAdayxgaLu: \eng{the organ fails when the wind is
 exhausted} oLagina gALi mugiduhoVdAga AgaRnf vAdayx
 niMtuhoVgutatxde. 

 \alnum{b} \kanmu\ AgaRnf yA itara gALi yA
 UduvAdayxvanunx Udalu kaqtakavAgi odagisida gALiparxvAha.
\num{6}
 (pArxNi \mo vu iruvudanunx yA hatitxradalilxruvudanunx sUcisuva)
 gALiyalilx sAgibaMda vAsane, gaMdha.
\num{7} (oMdara)
 parxcAra.
\num{8} hUsu; apAnavAyu.
\num{9} (ODuvAga yA satatavAgi
 sharxmapaDuvAga yA mAtADuvAga beVkAguva) usiru; damumx; tArxN;
 usirushakitx: \eng{have lost my wind} nanage
 usirillxdaMtAgide. \eng{smoking has affected his wind}
 dhUmapAnadiMda avanige usirADuvudu kaSaTxvAgide. 
\num{10} aLeLx;
 pakekx; ETu bidadxre tAtAkxlikavAgi shakitxhiVnavAguva edeya
 keLagina jAga: \eng{have one's wind taken} peTiTxniMda aLeLx yA
 usiru hiDidaMtAgu, damumx kaTiTxhoVgu.}}
 
\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{before the wind} gALiya baldiMda,
 veVgadiMda naDeyuva.
\num{2}\eng{between wind and water} gALi matutx
 niVrina naDuve; apAyada, dubaRl -- sithxtiyalilx, sAthxnadalilx;
 atatx dari itatx puli eMbaMte; uBaya saMkaTdalilx.
\num{3}
 \eng{break wind (} hUsu) biDu.
\num{4} \eng{broken wind} Edusiru;
 damumx; nitArxN.
\hypertarget{wind pagu5}{}
\num{5} \eng{close to the wind.} 

  \alnum{a} (nwkAyAnadalilx)
 (gALiya shakitxya upayoVgavanunx kaLedukoLaLxde) gALige AdaSuTx
 edurAgi. 

  \alnum{b} (\rUpa) ashilxVlteya, apArxmANikateya -- elelxyanunx
 samIpisi.  
\num{6} \eng{get (\engit{or} have) the wind up} (\AmA)
 hedaru; gAbariyAgu; digilubiVLu.
\num{7} \eng{get wind of } 

  \alnum{a} vAsane hiDi. 

  \alnum{b} Uhisu; shaMkisu. 

  \alnum{c} sudidx, vadaMti -- keVLu. 
\num{8}
 \eng{how (\engit{or} which way) the wind blows (\engit{or} lies)}
 (\rUpa) 

 \alnum{a}
 saMdaBaRgaLu heVgive; EneVnu vidayxmAnagaLu
 saMBavisabahudu.
 
\alnum{b} yArayAra aBipArxyagaLu, jnABipArxyagaLu
 heVgeheVge ive?
\num{9}\eng{in the wind} (\rUpa) Agutitxruva yA
 AgabahudAda; saMBavisiruva yA saMBavisabahudAda. 
\num{10} \eng{in
 the wind's eye} gALige neVredurAgi. 
\num{11} \eng{like the wind}
 gALiveVgadalilx; ati veVgavAgi; birusAgi. 
\num{12} \eng{near the wind} = \hyperlink{wind pagu5}{\pagu\ \eng{(5)}.}
\num{13} \eng{off the wind} (\nw)
 gALidikakxnunx biTuTx; sarAgavAgi (sAgutatx). 
\num{14} \eng{on a
 wind} (\nw) gALi biVsuva dikikxge, gALige -- edurAgi. 
\num{15}
 \eng{on the wind} (shabadx, vAsane, \mo vugaLa \vi) (oMdeDeyiMda
 inonxMdeDege) gALiyalilx -sAgutatx, haraDutatx,
 parxsAravAgutatx. 
\num{16} \eng{put the wind up} (\AmA)
 (\ashi) hedarisu; gAbarigoLisu. 
\num{17} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_r.pdf}{R}{raise(1) pagu(16)}{${}^1$raise} the wind.}
 \num{18} \eng{second wind } 

 \alnum{a} (vAyxyAma mADuvAga tegedukoLuLxva)
 damumx. 

 \alnum{b} (EnanAnxdarU mADalu) hosa shakitx. 
 \num{19}
 \eng{sound in limb and wind} pUNR(utatxma) AroVgayx
 sithxtiyalilx. 
\num{20} \eng{take (\engit{or} get) wind} sudidx -- ELu,
 habaubx, haraDu, parxsAravAgu. 
\num{21} \eng{take the wind out of a
 (person's) sails} (obabxna kirxye, mAtu, vAda, vicAra, \mo vanunx)
 tAneV modalu Uhisi yA upayoVgisikoMDu (avananunx) -- soVlisu,
 BaMgagoLisu.
\num{22} \eng{to the (four) winds} 

 \alnum{a} elAlx dikikxnalUlx; elelxDegU. 

 \alnum{b} upeVkeSxge yA nilaRkaSxyXkekx oLagAgi. 
\num{23} \eng{wind and weather} gALi maLegaLa hoDetakekx
 sikikx. 
\num{24} \eng{wind is in that quarter} parisithxti hAguMTu;
 viSaya A sithxtiyalilxde. 
\num{25} \eng{wind (\engit{or} winds) of change}
 (\rUpa) hosagALi; hosa badalAvaNegaLatatx, sudhAraNegaLa kaDege
 Oluva parxvaqtitx, parxBAva.}

\bentry
\word[wind(2)]{wind}
\pron{viMDf}
\gl{\sakirx}
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} vAsaneyiMda kaMDuhiDi: \eng{hounds wind
 foxes} beVTenAyigaLu narigaLanunx vAsaneyiMda
 kaMDuhiDiyutatxve.
\num{2} (vAyxyAmadiMda ALavAgi, beVgabeVgane)
 usiru biDuvaMte mADu; Edu barisu; Edisu; damumx barisu: \eng{give
 horse a gallop to wind him} kudurege Edu barisalu adanunx
 nAgAloVTdalilx ODisu.
\num{3} AyAsadiMda yA ETiniMda usirubiDu.
\num{4} (vishArxMtiyiMda) damumx tegeduko; usireLeduko;
 AyAsa, susutx -- hoVgalADisu: \eng{stopped to wind the horse}
 kudureyanunx damumx tegedukoLaLxlu nililxsida.
\num{5} AhAra koTTx
 naMtara (maguvanunx) teVgisu, teVguvaMte mADu. 
\num{6} (\ucAcx\ veYMDf) (\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{winded} \ucAcx\ veYMDiDf yA
 \eng{wound} \ucAcx\ vwMDf). (\kAparx) (koMbau, kahaLe, \mo vanunx)
 Udu; (Udi) dhavxni mADu.}

\bentry
\word[wind(3)]{wind}
\pron{viMDf}
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{ 
\num{1} baLasi dAri mADikoMDu hoVgu: \eng{the
 brook winds its way} hoLe sutitx baLasi hoVgutatxde. 
\num{2} (obabxra pirxVti \mo vugaLigAgi) hosedukoMDu hoVgu: \eng{he wound
 his way into my affection} avanu heVgoV hosedukoMDu nananx
 vishAvxsa gaLisida. 
\num{3} suruLi sututx; siMbiyAgi sututx:
 \eng{wind wool into ball} uNeNxdAravanunx uMDeyAgi sututx. 
\num{4} (rATe \mo vugaLige) dAra sututx. 
\num{5} (uNeNxdAra \mo vanunx) lDi,
 piMjiyiMda uMDe sututx. 
\num{6} sututx; sututxgaTuTx; apipxko;
 tabibxko; AliMgisu: \eng{wound the blanket round him} kaMbaLiyanunx
 meYyige sutitxkoMDa. \eng{wound her arms round the child} maguvanunx
 (toVLiniMda) bAci tabibxkoMDaLu. 
\num{7} (bauguriya) sutatxlU dArasututx. 
\num{8} (etutxyaMtarx \mo vanunx) sutitxsi, tirugisi -- seVdu, etutx:
 \eng{wind ore up from mine} gaNiyiMda aduranunx seVdi 
 etutx, seVdi meVlkekx tege. 
\num{9} (gaDiyAra \mo vakekx) kiVli
 koDu.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} sutitxkoMDu, sututxsutAtxgi, suruLi
 suruLiyAgi, aMkuDoMkAgi -- hoVgu, calisu: \eng{the river winds} nadi
 sutitx sutitx hoVgutatxde. 
\num{2} (uNeNx \mo vugaLa \vi)
 ceMDAguvaMte sutitxko; uMDe sutitxko: \eng{the wool winds into a
 ball} uNeNxyu ceMDinaMte sutitxkoLuLxtatxde. 
\num{3} sutitxko:
 \eng{the creeper winds round the pole} baLiLx kaMbada sutatx
 sutitxkoLuLxtatxde.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{winding staircase} sutitxhoVguva
 meTiTxlu sAlu; suruLi meTiTxlugaLu. 
\num{2} \eng{wind down}
 
 \alnum{a} (yaMtarxvayxvasethxya \vi, sutitxruvudanunx) biDisi
 keLagiLisu. 

 \alnum{b} (sutitx) keLagiLisu (\rUpa\ saha).
 
\alnum{c} (vayxkitxya \vi) viramisu; vishArxMti tegeduko. 

 \alnum{d}
 karxmeVN mucucx. 
\num{3} \eng{wind off} (sutitxruvudanunx) bicicx
 matetx sututx yA sutitxruvudanunx bicucx. 
\num{4} \eng{wind round
 one's finger} (obabxnanunx) sulBavAgi hatoVTiyalilx iTuTxkoMDiru;
 heVgeMdare hAge ADisu; kiruberaLalilx kuNisu. 
\num{5} \eng{wind up}

 \alnum{a} siMbi yA suruLi pUtiR sututx; suruLiyanunx yA siMbiyanunx
 bigimADu, bigiyAgi sututx. 

 \alnum{b} (\rUpa) (bigi, tiVvarxte,
 sAmathaRyx, \mo vanunx) hecicxsu; bigimADu: \eng{expectation was
 wound up to a high pitch} nirikeSxVyu tiVvarxteya unanxta sAthxyi
 muTiTxtu. 

 \alnum{c} konemuTiTxsu; mukAtxya -- Agu, mADu; kone -- muTuTx yA
 muTiTxsu: \eng{he wound up his speech declaring} -- eMdu 
 GoVSisi avanu tananx BASaN mukAtxyagoLisida. 

 \alnum{d} (vAyxpAra saMsethxyanunx) mucicxbiDu. 

 \alnum{e} (vAyxpAra saMsethxya \vi)
 mucicx divALiyAgu, pAparAgu. 

 \alnum{f} (\AmA) aMtimavAgi, baMdu -- seVru, talupu, biVLu: \eng{he
will wind up in prison} avanu konege jeYlige (baMdu) biVLutAtxne.  

 \alnum{g} (dArada tuMDu \mo vanunx)
 pUtiRyAgi siMbi sututx. 

 \alnum{h} (\kanmu\ gaDiyArada) taMti
 suruLiyanunx yA suruLi sutitxda taMtiyanunx bigimADu.}

\bentry

\pron{viMgf} 
\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (pakiSx, bAvali yA
 kiVTda) rekekx; pakaSx. 
\num{2} (hArada kelvu kirxmikiVTgaLa)
 rekekxge samanAda aMga, BAga. 
\num{3} vimAnada rekekx; rekekxyaMtha
 adara sahAyaka BAga. 
\num{4} (kaTTxDa, seYnayxvUyxha, \mo vugaLa)
 pAshaRvx; kakeSx; pakakx; horacAcida BAga: \eng{north wing was added in
 17th century} (kaTTxDada) utatxra pAshaRvxvanunx 17neya
 shatamAnadalilx seVrisalAyitu. \eng{cavalry was massed on left wing}
 ashavxdaLavanunx balpakakxdalilx jmAyisalAyitu. 
\num{5} (\bava

 pakakxgaLu. 
\num{6} (\birx) moVTArf vAhanada cakarxda
 kesarutaDe.

 \alnum{b} ATda meYdAnada
 pakakxBAga.

 GaTkagaLu. 
\num{10} (\bava dalilx) (\eng{RAF} daLa \mo vugaLalilx)
 vimAna cAlkana gurutu bilelx: \eng{get one's wings} gurutina bilelx
 paDe.

 pAshaRvxBAga, horacAcu.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu}

\num{1} \eng{clip (person's) wings .}

 \alnum{a} (vayxkitxya) kAyaRcaTuvaTikegaLanunx kuMThitagoLisu,
 siVmitagoLisu. 

 \alnum{b} (vayxkitxya) mahatAvxkAMkeSxgaLige taDe
 oDuDx. 

 \alnum{c} (vayxkitxya) haNkAsina sAvxtaMtarxyXvanunx
 moTkugoLisu; (vayxkitxya) KcuRvecacx KoVtA mADu. 
\num{2} \eng{(come)
 on the wings of wind} vAyuveVgadalilx (bA). 
\num{3} \eng{lend (\engit{or}
 give) wings to} vayxkitxyanunx yA vasutxvanunx tavxregoLisu,
 beVga AguvaMte mADu. 
\num{4} \eng{on a wing and a prayer}
 yashasisxna tiVrA alpx avakAsha hoMdi. 
\num{5}\eng{on the wing}
 hArutatx; calisutatx; parxyANdalilx. 
\hyperdef{W}{wing(1) pagu(6)}{}

 one's wings} (\rUpa) saMpUNR shakitxsAmathaRyx beLesiko;
 shakitxsAdhayxte garigedaruvaMte mADu. 
\num{7} \eng{sprout wings}
 rekekx mUDisu; shakitx moLeyisu: \eng{his wings are sprouting}

 avanalilxruva deVvatA guNgaLu, shakitxgaLu parxkaTvAgutitxve. 
\hyperdef{W}{wing(1) pagu(8)}{}

 \eng{take under one's wing} (obabxna) poVSaNe vahisiko; rakaSxNe
 horu; AsharxyakoDu.

 meVleVru.

 (obabxna meVle) horisu; AroVpisu.}}

 Baya nanagide.
\num{3} \eng{wish for} (oMdakAkxgi) Ase paDu yA Ase
 vayxkatxpaDisu.
\num{4} \eng{wish I were a bird} nAnoMdu
 hakikxyAgidadxre (cenAnxgitutx).
\num{5} \eng{wish oneself dead}
 (tAnu) satutxhoVgidadxre cenAnxgitutx eMduko.
\num{6}\eng{wish
 (person) good day} (vayxkitxge) dinada shuBakAmane koVru.
\num{7}
 \eng{wish person \hyperref{kandict_j.pdf}{J}{joy(1) nuga}{${}^1$joy} of} .
\num{8}\eng{wishes me well} nanage
 shuBavAgali enunxtAtxne.
\num{9} \eng{wishes well to all men} sakal

 yArigU keDuku bayasuvudillx.}
