 (paMdayx, kAyARcaraNe, sAthxna, \mo vugaLiMda) hiMtegeduko
 : \eng{withdraw the horse from the race} paMdayxdiMda kudureyanunx
 hiMtegeduko. \eng{withdraw the troops from the front}
 yudadhxBUmiyiMda seYnayxvanunx hiMtegeduko, vApasu karesu.
\num{6}
 (bAyxMkiniMda, KAteyiMda)haN hiMtegeduko: \eng{withdraw money from
 bank} bAyxMkiniMda haN hiMpaDe.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\akirx} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} hiMsari; vApasAgu; hiMdakekx baru;
 viramisu: \eng{withdraw from the race} paMdayxdiMda hinasxri;
 sapxdheRyiMda viramisu.
\num{2} (sathxLadiMda, sAthxnadiMda) horaTuhoVgu; nigaRmisu.}}

\num{2} hoTeTxbAka yA durAseya vayxkitx.
\num{3} (\ashi) toVLa;
 mitimiVrida kAmuka parxvaqtitxyavanu; heMgasaranunx kADi
 keDisuvavanu; lMpaT.
\num{4} (\saM)
 
 \alnum{a} (piTiVlu \mo\ kamAnu -- vAdayxgaLalilxna) kelvu
 savxragaLalilx baruva kakaRsha shabadx. 

 \alnum{b} kelvu haLeya AgaRnf vAdayxgaLalilxna taMti

 eDavaTuTx taMduko.

 hiDididadxrU kaSaTx, biTTxrU kaSaTx eMba ikakxTiTxnalilxru.
\num{3}

 tapipxsiko; dAridarxyx mAri maneyoLakekx hogada hAge noVDiko.
\num{4}

 mADuvudakekx hecucx iSaTxpaDuva vayxkitx.

 wolves} dayAdAkiSxNyxvillxde (obabx vayxkitx \mo varanunx)
 balikoDu.

 sariyAgi baMdididxVye.

\gl{\nA} 
{\dictmeaning{

 pada; nuDi; solulx: \eng{is not the word for it} adakekx takakx
 padavallx.

 baLasuva, mUlBUta aBivayxkitxya GaTka, aMsha.
\num{3} mAtu; BASaN:
 \eng{honest in word and deed} nuDiyalilx matutx naDeyalilx
 pArxmANika; nuDidaMte naDeyuva (niSeThxyuLaLx). 
\num{4} (\bava\ yA
 \Eva dalilx) heVLida mAtu; heVLike; nuDi; TiVke; ukitx; vacana;
 mAtukate.
\num{5} (\bava dalilx) mAtu; hADina sAhitayx, naTna
 mAtugaLu, \mo vu.
\num{6} (keVval bAyimAtinalilx) heVLidudu; mAtu;

 mAtinallxSeTxV dheYyaRshAli.

 \eng{send word} samAcAra kaLuhisu.
\num{8} ADida mAtu; koTTx vacana;
 vAgAdxna: \eng{gave us their word} avaru vAgAdxna mADidaru, mAtu
 koTTxru.
\num{9} Ajecnx; apapxNe; shAsana: \eng{his word is law}
 avana mAteV shAsana.

\num{11} sUkitx;
 dheyxVya(pada). 
\num{12} (\bava dalilx) koVpada mAtu; jgaLa:
 \eng{have words with} koVpadiMda -- nuDi, kUgADu.}}

\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{

 mADutatxde? \eng{your idea does not work} ninanx aBipArxya
 kAyaRkAriyAgillx.
\num{6} (yaMtarxBAgada \vi) ODu; ADu; naDe;
 tirugu; kelsa mADu: \eng{wheel works freely} cakarx sarAgavAgi
 tirugutatxde.
\num{7} kaSaTxdiMda yA nidhAnavAgi -- calisu, sAgu,
 muMduvare: \eng{work upstream} nadiya meVlumuKvAgi hoVgu.
\num{8}
 (satata calneyiMda) karxmeVN saDil, aLaLxka, \mo vu Agu 
\num{9}
 kuSxbadhxvAgu (\rUpa\ saha): \eng{face worked violently} muK
 tiVvarxvAgi parxkuSxbadhxvAyitu. 
\num{10} (nwkeya \vi) gALige
 virudadhxvAgi, edurAgi -- sAgu, hoVgu.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{set to work} 

 \alnum{a} kelsakekx keYhacucx,
 toDagu; kelsa pArxraMBisu. 

 \alnum{b} kelsakekx hacucx, toDagisu;
 kelsa pArxraMBa mADuvaMte mADu.
\num{2}\eng{work an idea to death}
 (yAvudAdarU vicAra \mo vanunx) atiyAgi, savakalAguvaMte
 baLasu.
\num{3} \eng{work away (\engit{or} on)} (biDade) kelsa -- mADutitxru,
 muMduvaresu.
\num{4} \eng{work in} (nidashaRna, saMgati, \mo vanunx)
 heVgoV oLakekx tUrisu; sathxLa mADi, avakAsha kalipxsi, oLakekx --
 heNe, neVyi, seVrisu. 
\num{5} \eng{work one's fingers to the
\hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bone(1) nuga(13)}{${}^1$bone}.}
\num{6} \eng{work one's \hyperref{kandict_p.pdf}{P}{passage(1) pagu(2)}{${}^1$passage}.}
\num{7} \eng{work it} (\AmA) sAdhisu; uMTumADu; udidxSaTx PalitAMsha paDe.
\num{8}\eng{work off} 

  \alnum{a} kelsa mADi -- nivArisiko, pariharisiko, tiVrisiko,
 kaLeduko, kaDame mADiko: \eng{works his bad temper on his servants}
 tananx koVpavanunx ALugaLa meVle tiVrisikoLuLxtAtxne, ALugaLa meVle
 koVpa toVrisi nivArisikoLuLxtAtxne. \eng{worked off his debt} duDidu
 tananx sAl tiVrisikoMDa. \eng{work off excess of weight} atiyAda
 tUkavanunx kaLeduko, kaDame mADiko. 

 \alnum{b} (vasutxgaLige girAki
 \mo varanunx hoMdisi) mArihAku; vileVvAri mADu: \eng{worked off}
 \eng{3000} \eng{copies} mUrusAvira parxtigaLanunx mArihAkida.
\num{9}
 \eng{work one's will} (\AmA) tananx udedxVsha sAdhisiko,
 IDeVrisiko.
\num{10} \eng{work out} 

 \alnum{a} (gaNitada) lekakxmADu;
 lekakxkekx utatxra kaMDuhiDi; lekakxda parxshenx biDisu. 

 \alnum{b}
 motatx kaMDuhiDi; eNisu. 

 \alnum{c} motatx Agu: \eng{the total works
 out at Rs. 2000} lekAkxcAradalilx, motatxdalilx adu $2000$
 rUpAyigaLAgutatxde. 

 \alnum{d} (lekakxda \vi) mADalAgu; mADabaru;
 nidiRSaTx PalitAMsha niVDu: \eng{this sum will not work out} I
 lekakxvanunx mADalAguvudillx.

 \alnum{e} vishiSaTx PalitAMsha
 hoMdiru: \eng{the plan worked out well} yoVjne
 saPalvAyitu. 

 \alnum{f} vivaragaLanunx aNigoLisu; kUlMkaSavAgi
 yoVjisu: \eng{has worked out a scheme} yoVjneyoMdanunx
 tayArisidAdxne.

 \alnum{g} parxyatanxpaTuTx, kaSaTxpaTuTx -- sAdhisu,
 gaLisu, paDe: \eng{worked out one's salvation} parxyatanx mADi
 tananx mukitx sAdhisikoMDa.

 \alnum{h} kelsadiMda -- baridAgu,
 KAliyAgu: \eng{the mine is worked out} toVDitoVDi gaNi
 KAliyAgide. 

 \alnum{i} kelsadiMda -- susAtxgu, baLalu, AyAsa hoMdu:
 \eng{the person is worked out} avanu duDidu
 susAtxgidAdxne. 

 \alnum{j} deYhika vAyxyAmadalilx toDagu 
\num{11}
 \eng{work over} 

 \alnum{a} pUtiR, AdayxMtavAgi -- pariVkiSxsu, taniKe
 mADu. 

 \alnum{b} (\AmA) keYmADu; baDi; cacucx. 
\num{12}\eng{work to
 rule} (\kanmu\ keYgArikA keVSxtarxdalilx utapxnanx matutx dakaSxte

\BU). (\kanmu\ keLagina saMdaBaRgaLalilx baLake): 
\num{1} divxtiVya matutx parxthama puruSagaLalilx, matutx kelavomemx
utatxma puruSadalUlx saha \eng{=
\hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{should(1)}{should(1):}}    

 \alnum{a} paroVkaSx varadiyalilx:
 \eng{he said he would be home by evening} sAyaMkAlda hotitxge
 manege baruveneMdu avanu heVLida. 

 \alnum{b} saMBAvanAsUcaka
 kirxyeyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{they would have been killed if they had
 gone} oMdu veVLe avaru hoVgididxdadxre avaru
 koleyAgutitxdadxru.
\num{2} rUDhiya yA dinaMparxtiya kelsavanunx
 sUcisalu: \eng{would wait for her every evening} parxtidina saMje
 avaLigAgi kAyutitxdadx.
\num{3} parxshenx yA namarx beVDikeyanunx
 sUcisalu: \eng{would they like it?} adanunx avaru
 iSaTxpaDuvareV? \eng{would you come in, please?} dayaviTuTx, oLage
 baruvirA?
\num{4} saMBavaniVyateyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{I guess she
 would be over fifty by now} sadayxkekx Ake aivatatxnunx
 dATidAdxLeMdu nananx Uhe.
\num{5} (sAhitayxka) iSaTxvanunx sUcisalu:
 \eng{would that you were here} niVvu ililx iruvaMtAdare nanage
 cenAnxgirutitxtutx.
\num{6} opipxgeyanunx sUcisalu: \eng{they would
 not help} avaru sahAya mADuvudillx, mADalopupxvudillx.}
\eentry

\bentry

\gl{\kirx} (\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{wrapped}; \vakaq\
 \eng{wrapping}).

\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} (kAgada \mo vugaLiMda)
 sututx; sutitxDu; hodisu; mucucx; AcACxdisu: \eng{wrap it in paper}
 kAgadadalilx sututx.
\num{2} (\rUpa) (hima, atiyAda mAtu, rahasayx,
 \mo vugaLiMda) Avarisu; AcACxdisu; mucucx; mucicxru: \eng{affair is
 wrapped in mystery} saMgati rahasayxdalilx mucicxkoMDide,
 AcACxditavAgide.
\num{3} hodisu; mucucx; cenAnxgi sututx:
 \eng{wrapped her shawl closer about her} avaLu tananx shAlnunx
 cenAnxgi hodudxkoMDaLu.
\num{4} (\ashi) (vAhanada \vi) niMtiruva
 vasutxvige -- gududx, DikikxhoDe, saMGaTiTxsu.}}
 
\noindent

\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{wrap over} (uDupina \vi) dharisidAga
 (oMdara meVloMdu hodisidaMte) mucicx hoVgu 
\num{2} \eng{wrap up} 

 \alnum{a}
 hodudxko; (meY \mo vanunx) mucicxko: \eng{mind you, wrap up well if
 you go out} joVke, niVnu horage hoVdare, becacxge
 hodeduko. 

 \alnum{b} (\ashi, AjAcnxthaRka) tepapxgiru; sumamxniru.
 
\alnum{c} mugisibiDu; itayxthaR mADu.
\num{3} \eng{wrap up meaning}
 athaR mucicxbiDu; jTilvAgisu: \eng{he wraps up his meaning in
 tortuous sentences} avanu tananx mAtina athaRvanunx aMkuDoMkAgi
 tirucida vAkayxgaLalilx mucicxDutAtxne.
\num{4} \eng{wrapped up}
 maganxvAgiru; talilxVnavAgiru; muLugiru: \eng{the mother is wrapped
 up in her child} tAyi maguvina keSxVmapoVSaNegaLalilx
 maganxLAgidAdxLe.}

\bentry
\word[wreck(1)]{wreck} 
\pron{rekf} 
\gl{\nA} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} hALu; (vi)nAsha; dhavxMsa: \eng{the wreck of his happiness} avana 
suKda vinAsha.
\num{2} nwkAGAta; haDagoDeyuvudu. 
\num{3} Cidarx, Baganx -- nwke; oDeda haDagu: \eng{the 
 shores are strewn with wrecks} daDada 
 meVlelAlx haDagina BagAnxvasheVSagaLu, oDeda 
 cUrugaLu celAlxpililxyAgi bididxve.
\num{4} shithil, Baganx, hALAda, jiVNR, jjRrita, murukalu, 
 dhavxMsavAda -- kaTTxDa, manuSayx, vasutx: \eng{had become a physical
 and mental wreck}  
 deYhikavAgi matutx mAnasikavAgi jjRritavAgi 
 hoVgidAdxne. \eng{a wreck of his former self} 
 tananx pUvaRsithxtiya perxVtavAgidAdxne.

{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} bare; leVKisu: \eng{does not read or
 write} Odalu yA bareyalu bAradu.
\num{2} (leVKna \mo vugaLanunx)
 bareyuvudaralilx toDagiru; bareyuva vaqtitx hiDidiru: \eng{writes
 for the local newspaper} sathxLiVya patirxkege
 bareyutAtxne.
\num{3} kAgada, patarx baredu (vayxkitxge) kaLuhisu.}}
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1}\eng{nothing to write \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{home(3) nuga(5)}{${}^3$home} about.}
\num{2}
\eng{write down} 

 \alnum{a} barediDu; dAKle mADu; barehadalilx
 dAKlisu. 

 \alnum{b} (Odu, bareha, aMtasutx, \mo vugaLalilx keLa
 aMtasitxnavarigAgiyoV eMbaMte) tiLiyAgi, saraLiVkarisi bare;
 tagigxsi bare. 

 \alnum{c} jredu, haLidu yA lAGavavAgi
 bare. 

 \alnum{d} (baMDavALa patarx, sarakugaLu, \mo vugaLa) muKbele,
 namUdubele -- tagigxsu, kaDamemADu.
\num{3} \eng{write in}

 \alnum{a} saMsethxyoMdakekx (\kanmu\ AkAshavANi parxsAra nilyakekx salhe,
 sUcane, parxshenx, \mo vanunx) bare; baredu, liKitarUpadalilx
 tiLisu. 

 \alnum{b} (\ame) matacunAvaNeyalilx aBayxthiRgaLa paTiTxge
 (hecicxna yA biTuTxhoVgiruva) hesarugaLanunx
 seVrisu.
\num{4}\eng{write into} (ucita badalAvaNegaLoMdige) (hosa
 viSaya yA parxsaMgavanunx) seVrisu.
\num{5} \eng{write large}
 dapapxnAgi, doDaDxdAgi, edudxkANuvaMte -- bare.
\num{6}\eng{write off.} 
 
\alnum{a} kAgada baredu ravAne mADu, kaLuhisu. 

 \alnum{b} (vasUlAgada sAl, kaLeduhoVda sAmAnu, \mo vugaLa) dAKleyanunx -
 aLisihAku, hoDeduhAku; vajA mADu; (baMDavALa, Asitx, sAmAnu, \mo
 vugaLa) naSaTxvanunx yA matetx paDeyalAgadiruvikeyanunx opipxko,
 dAKle mADu. 

 \alnum{c} (vAhana \mo vanunx) ripeVri mADalAgadaSuTx
 nAshagoLisu, hALumADu. 

 \alnum{d} saliVsAgi bare; liVlAjAlvAgi
 racisu.
\num{7} \eng{write out} 

 \alnum{a} pUtiRyAgi yA pUNRrUpadalilx
 bare; AdayxMtavAgi namUdisu, nirUpisu. 

 \alnum{b} baredu
 susAtxgu: \eng{have written myself out} baredubaredu
 susAtxgidedxVne, bareyuvudakekx beVreVnU viSayavillxdavanAgidedxVne. 
\num{8}\eng{write out of} bareda kaqtiyiMda (pAtarx,
 GaTne, \mo vanunx) kitutx hAku; aLisi hAku.
\num{9} \eng{writes a
 good hand} suMdaravAgi bareyutAtxne; avana keYbaraha, akaSxragaLu
 mudAdxgive. 
\num{10} \eng{write up} 

 \alnum{a} (GaTne \mo vugaLa bagegx)
 pUNRvAgi bare; pUtiRvivaragaLanunx nirUpisu, koDu. 

 \alnum{b} hogaLi, koMDADi, parxshaMsisi -- bare. 

 \alnum{c} (dinacari pusatxka
 \mo vugaLalilx) dAKlegaLanunx sadayxdavarege barediDu,
 tahalfvarege taru.} 
\eentry

\bentry
\word[wrong(1)]{wrong} 
\pron{rAMgf} 
\gl{\gu} 
{\dictmeaning{
\num{1} tapApxda; keTuTxhoVda; vayxtayxsatxvAda; karxmatapipxda;
avayxvasethxya; susithxtiyalilxllxda: \eng{something is wrong with
him} avanalilx EnoV vayxtAyxsavAgide. \eng{something is wrong with my
heart} nananx haqdaya susithxtiyalilxllx. \eng{my watch has gone
wrong} nananx gaDiyAra keTuTxhoVgide. 
\num{2} tapApxda; sariyallxda; nijsithxtigiMta yA vAsatxva
saMgatigiMta BinanxvAda: \eng{gave a wrong answer} tapu px utatxra
koTTx.  
\num{3} tapApxda; beVkillxda; beVDavAda; anapeVkiSxtavAda;
opipxgeyAgada : \eng{the wrong road} tapu px rasetx; beVkirada
rasetx. \eng{a wrong decision} tapu px tiVmARna; yukitxyukatxvAgirada,
opipxgeyAgada -- tiVmARna.  
\num{4} tapApxda; ucitavallxda; yukatxvallxda; takukxdallxda: \eng{he
always says the wrong thing} avanu yAvAgalU ayukatxvAdudanenxV
heVLutAtxne. 
\num{5} anAyxyada; adhamaRda; duSaTx; pApada; keTTxdAda; kAnUnige yA
niVtige virudadhxvAda: \eng{it is wrong to steal} kadiyuvudu
keTTxdudx. \eng{took the wrong way} keTTxdAri, anAyxyada mAgaR
hiDida. \eng{a wrong deed} pApakaqtayx; duSaTxkAyaR. 
\num{6} kAyaR, tiVmARna yA vidhAnadalilx -- sariyallxda, sariyAgirada:
\eng{you are wrong to blame him} niVnu avananunx bayuyxvudu sariyallx,
tapupx.}} 
 
\noindent
\gl{\pagu} 
\dictmeaning{
\num{1} \eng{get (\engit{or} hold of) the wrong end of the stick} (\rUpa)
athaRmADikoLuLxvalilx pUtiR tapupxmADu, tapApxgiru; saMpUNRvAgi
tapapxthaR mADiko. 
\num{2}\eng{get on the wrong side of} (obabxna) avagarxhakekx,
avakaqpege -- biVLu, pAtarxnAgu.  
\num{3} \eng{go down the wrong way} (AhAra) ananxnALakekx badalAgi
shAvxsanALakekx hoVgu; tapu pxnALadoLakekx iLi. 
\num{4} \eng{in the wrong box} 

 \alnum{a} kilxSaTx parisithxtiyalilx. 

 \alnum{b} parxtikUl parisithxtiyalilx. 

 \alnum{c} ikakxTiTxna yA peVcina yA mujugarada parisithxtiyalilx. 
\num{5} \eng{on the wrong side of} 

 \alnum{a} (vayxkitxya) avakaqpege oLagAda. 

 \alnum{b} (heVLida, namUdisida vayasisxgiMta) savxlpx hecAcxgiruva.
\num{6} \eng{(the) wrong way round} rUDhiya yA yukatxvAda mAgaRkekx, daqSiTxkoVnakekx -- edurina yA virudadhxvAda mAgaR yA daqSiTxkoVna.
\num{7}\eng{what is wrong with...?} (\AmA) adaralelxVnu doVSa, tapipxde? (adakekx badaliyAgi beVre yAvudaradU agatayxvillx eMbathaRdalilx) adeVke -- beVDa, kUDadu?
\num{8} \eng{wrong side out} oLa(muK) horagAgiruva.}
\eentry
